</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>When they entered the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> classroom they found Professor Umbridge already seated at the teacher’s desk, wearing the fluffy pink cardigan of the night before and the black velvet bow on top of her head. <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> was again reminded forcibly of a large fly perched unwisely on top of an even larger <a href="/wiki/Toad" title="Toad">toad</a>.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;A negative impression of Dolores<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p><b>Madam Dolores Jane Umbridge</b> (b. <a href="/wiki/26_August" title="26 August">26 August</a>, <a href="/wiki/1965" title="1965">1965</a> or earlier)<sup id="cite_ref-birth_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-birth-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> was a <a href="/wiki/Half-blood" title="Half-blood">half-blood</a><sup id="cite_ref-pottermoreprofile_1-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermoreprofile-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">witch</a> and a <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">British Ministry of Magic</a> bureaucrat who served as <a href="/wiki/Senior_Undersecretary_to_the_Minister_for_Magic" title="Senior Undersecretary to the Minister for Magic">Senior Undersecretary to the Minister for Magic</a> under <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Magic" title="Minister for Magic">Ministers</a> <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rufus_Scrimgeour" title="Rufus Scrimgeour">Rufus Scrimgeour</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Pius_Thicknesse" title="Pius Thicknesse">Pius Thicknesse</a>.
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a> by order of the Ministry, she was installed as the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">Professor</a> at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a> and then later the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_High_Inquisitor" title="Hogwarts High Inquisitor">Hogwarts High Inquisitor</a> and <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmistress</a> of Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry, after Professor Albus Dumbledore had been fired. In all three of these positions at Hogwarts she had enormous power over the students, teachers, and the curriculum, which she wielded despotically.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Her time at Hogwarts was characterised by cruelty and abusive punishments against students and because of her interfering and condescending ways, she was widely despised by most students and teachers alike.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After her suspension from these additional posts and the <a href="/wiki/Fall_of_the_Ministry_of_Magic" title="Fall of the Ministry of Magic">fall of the Ministry of Magic</a>, Umbridge ran the <a href="/wiki/Muggle-Born_Registration_Commission" title="Muggle-Born Registration Commission">Muggle-Born Registration Commission</a> and sadistically prosecuted many innocent people.<sup id="cite_ref-DH13_5-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH13-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> After the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>, she was sentenced to <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> for her crimes against <a href="/wiki/Muggle-borns" class="mw-redirect" title="Muggle-borns">Muggle-borns</a>, where she would remain for the rest of her life.<sup id="cite_ref-imprisonment_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-imprisonment-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Biography">Biography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=1" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Biography">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Biography"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life">Early life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=2" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Early life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Early life"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Dolores Umbridge was the first child of a <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a> named <a href="/wiki/Orford_Umbridge" title="Orford Umbridge">Orford Umbridge</a> and a <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> named <a href="/wiki/Ellen_Cracknell" title="Ellen Cracknell">Ellen Cracknell</a>. Her younger <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge%27s_brother" title="Dolores Umbridge&#39;s brother">brother</a> was a <a href="/wiki/Squib" title="Squib">Squib</a>, but Dolores was born a witch. Under her father's influence, she despised her Muggle mother and her Squib brother, considering them inferior to her and her father, and Dolores and her father denounced them. Before Dolores reached 15 years old, Ellen and her son returned to the Muggle world, never to be heard of again.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermoreprofile_1-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermoreprofile-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At some point she obtained <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge%27s_wand" title="Dolores Umbridge&#39;s wand">her wand</a>, made from <a href="/wiki/Birch" title="Birch">birch</a> and <a href="/wiki/Dragon_heartstring" title="Dragon heartstring">dragon heartstring</a> with an unusually short length of only eight inches. According to <a href="/wiki/Garrick_Ollivander" title="Garrick Ollivander">Garrick Ollivander</a>, abnormally short wands usually selected those whose moral character was stunted, rather than because they were physically short.<sup id="cite_ref-wandlength_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-wandlength-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hogwarts_years">Hogwarts years</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=3" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hogwarts years">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Hogwarts years"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On turning eleven, Umbridge started attending <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>. She was <a href="/wiki/Sorting_ceremony" title="Sorting ceremony">Sorted</a> into <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> and her head of house was <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Slytherin_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Slytherin-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> She did not have a good relationship with Slughorn, who considered her to be an "idiotic woman" and that he "never liked her".<sup id="cite_ref-HBP4_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP4-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> She was also never given any position of power (i.e. <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">Prefect</a>, <a href="/wiki/Head_Boy_or_Girl" title="Head Boy or Girl">Head Girl</a>) during her studies, which made her feel deprived, and she never truly enjoyed her time as a student at Hogwarts.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermoreprofile_1-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermoreprofile-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_at_the_Ministry">Career at the Ministry</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=4" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Career at the Ministry">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Career at the Ministry"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Ascension">Ascension</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=5" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Ascension">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Ascension"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>...she drafted an anti-werewolf legislation two years ago that makes it almost impossible for him [Lupin] to get a job.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> discussing Umbridge's anti-werewolf laws<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>After leaving Hogwarts, Umbridge quickly rose to influential positions in the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">British Ministry of Magic</a>. She started her political career as an intern in the <a href="/wiki/Improper_Use_of_Magic_Office" title="Improper Use of Magic Office">Improper Use of Magic Office</a>. Before reaching age 30, she became the Head of the Office, evidence of her ruthless tactics under her sweet attitude, which also involved taking credit for other people's work. This set up the beginning of her dubious career as a Ministry employee, one who tyrannised her subordinates while flattering her equals and her superiors.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermoreprofile_1-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermoreprofile-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p class="mw-empty-elt"></p><figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cc/Dolores_Umbridge_sign.png/revision/latest?cb=20151128185353" class="image"><img alt="Dolores Umbridge sign.png" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="93" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dolores Umbridge sign.png" data-image-key="Dolores_Umbridge_sign.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cc/Dolores_Umbridge_sign.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20151128185353" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cc/Dolores_Umbridge_sign.png/revision/latest?cb=20151128185353" class="image"><img alt="Dolores Umbridge sign.png" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cc/Dolores_Umbridge_sign.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20151128185353" decoding="async" width="250" height="93" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dolores Umbridge sign.png" data-image-key="Dolores_Umbridge_sign.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cc/Dolores_Umbridge_sign.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20151128185353" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dolores_Umbridge_sign.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 	</figcaption> </figure><p>
Dolores, being very opportunistic and power-hungry, was ashamed of her father, who was a low-level worker in the <a href="/wiki/Magical_Maintenance_Department" title="Magical Maintenance Department">Department of Magical Maintenance</a>, while she was seeking a professional career. Under her pressure, he retired early and she promised him a small monthly allowance in exchange for quietly leaving the public sight. From that point on she lied about her family, claiming that she was a <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood" title="Pure-blood">pure-blood</a> rather than a half-blood. She eventually became <a href="/wiki/Senior_Undersecretary_to_the_Minister_for_Magic%27s_office" title="Senior Undersecretary to the Minister for Magic&#39;s office">Senior Undersecretary</a> to the <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Magic" title="Minister for Magic">Minister for Magic</a> and had a place in the <a href="/wiki/Wizengamot" title="Wizengamot">Wizengamot</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermoreprofile_1-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermoreprofile-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p class="mw-empty-elt"></p><p>Whenever she was asked (usually by workmates who did not like her) 'are you related to that Umbridge who used to mop the floors here?', she would smile her sweetest, laugh, and deny any connection, claiming that her deceased father had been a distinguished member of the Wizengamot. Nasty things tended to happen to people who asked about Orford, or anything about which she did not like talking, and people who wanted to remain on her good side pretended to believe her version of her ancestry.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermoreprofile_1-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermoreprofile-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Throughout her career, Dolores tried to garner affections of one of her superiors in order to advance her status and security, with no particular desire on which superior it would be, as long as he would be a powerful husband. However, while they valued her hard work and ambition, those who got to know her best found it very difficult to like her very much. Indeed, when she got intoxicated from a glass of sweet <a href="/wiki/Sherry" title="Sherry">sherry</a>, Dolores was prone to spout very uncharitable views, which shocked even those of anti-Muggle ideologies with some of her suggestions, behind closed doors, of the treatment that the non-magical community deserved. As such, Dolores never succeeded in getting <a href="/wiki/Marriage" title="Marriage">married</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermoreprofile_1-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermoreprofile-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Umbridge's hatred towards "<a href="/wiki/Half-breed" title="Half-breed">half-breeds</a>" led her to draft a piece of <a href="/wiki/Anti-werewolf_legislation" title="Anti-werewolf legislation">anti-werewolf legislation</a> in <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a>, which made it nearly impossible for <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolves</a>, such as <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a>, to find work.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> This act also made it easier for Lord Voldemort to recruit werewolves to his cause, preying on their treatment by the Ministry. In <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>, she also campaigned that the <a href="/wiki/Merpeople" title="Merpeople">Merpeople</a> be rounded up and tagged, though this idea was scrapped due to it being too ludicrous to be put into effect.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Attack_in_Little_Whinging">Attack in Little Whinging</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=6" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Attack in Little Whinging">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Attack in Little Whinging"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Attack_in_Little_Whinging" title="Attack in Little Whinging">Attack in Little Whinging</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>I’m sure I must have misunderstood you, Professor Dumbledore. So silly of me. But it sounded for a teensy moment as though you were suggesting that the Ministry of Magic had ordered an attack on this boy!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Umbridge during Harry's hearing<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/Umbridge_hearing.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170817022544" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Umbridge hearing.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge_hearing.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/Umbridge_hearing.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170817022544" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/Umbridge_hearing.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170817022544" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/Umbridge_hearing.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170817022544" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Umbridge hearing.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge_hearing.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bb/Umbridge_hearing.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170817022544" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Umbridge_hearing.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Umbridge at Harry Potter's Disciplinary as a member of the Wizengamot</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As Senior Under-Secretary to the <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Magic" title="Minister for Magic">Minister for Magic</a> in <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, Umbridge managed to claw her way up to power using <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a>'s increasing paranoia and insecurities to her advantage.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermoreprofile_1-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermoreprofile-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>She also used her authority to intimidate <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> during <a href="/wiki/Disciplinary_hearing_of_Harry_Potter" title="Disciplinary hearing of Harry Potter">an interrogation</a> before the <a href="/wiki/Wizengamot" title="Wizengamot">Wizengamot</a>. She was very outspoken against him and tried to discredit his claim that the only reason he cast a Patronus Charm was because of the presence of Dementors.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>She said that the Dementors were under the control of the Ministry, and that it was preposterous that they would just happen to wander into a Muggle suburb and chance upon a wizard. She believed Harry should be punished for inadvertently violating the <a href="/wiki/Decree_for_the_Reasonable_Restriction_of_Underage_Sorcery" title="Decree for the Reasonable Restriction of Underage Sorcery">Decree for the Reasonable Restriction of Underage Sorcery</a>. Owing to the fairness of <a href="/wiki/Amelia_Bones" title="Amelia Bones">Madam Bones</a> and a majority ruling of the court, Harry was found innocent. Only <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Fudge</a>, Umbridge, and roughly a half-dozen of the court voted for conviction. Harry was cleared of all charges, much to Umbridge's disappointment.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/Harry_casts_Patronus_spell.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140616170354" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="120" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry casts Patronus spell.gif" data-image-key="Harry_casts_Patronus_spell.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/Harry_casts_Patronus_spell.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140616170354" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/Harry_casts_Patronus_spell.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140616170354" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/Harry_casts_Patronus_spell.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140616170354" decoding="async" width="245" height="120" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry casts Patronus spell.gif" data-image-key="Harry_casts_Patronus_spell.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/Harry_casts_Patronus_spell.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140616170354" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_casts_Patronus_spell.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Dementor attack that Umbridge ordered on Harry Potter</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>What Umbridge did not reveal at the time was that she herself had ordered the <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementor</a> attack on Harry and his cousin <a href="/wiki/Dudley_Dursley" title="Dudley Dursley">Dudley Dursley</a>, since both possible outcomes would work in the Ministry's favour. Harry would either be subjected to the Dementor's kiss or would be forced to conjure a <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a> to fend them off, which would give them an excuse to expel him. As a result, she was distraught that Harry "wriggled out of that one".<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Becoming_a_Hogwarts_professor">Becoming a Hogwarts professor</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=7" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Becoming a Hogwarts professor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Becoming a Hogwarts professor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>The Ministry of Magic has always considered the education of young witches and wizards to be of vital importance...There again, progress for progress's sake must be discouraged, for our tried and tested traditions often require no tinkering... Let us move forward, then, into a new era of openness, effectiveness, and accountability, intent on preserving what ought to be preserved, perfecting what needs to be perfected, and pruning wherever we find practices that ought to be prohibited.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Umbridge rudely interrupting Albus Dumbledore's start-of-term speech<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/08/Umbridge_speech.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160609132202" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="109" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Umbridge speech.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge_speech.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/08/Umbridge_speech.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160609132202" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/08/Umbridge_speech.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160609132202" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/08/Umbridge_speech.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160609132202" decoding="async" width="250" height="109" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Umbridge speech.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge_speech.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/08/Umbridge_speech.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160609132202" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Umbridge_speech.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dolores Umbridge interrupts <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> with a speech of her own, during the Start-of-Term Feast</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, Umbridge was placed at Hogwarts as the new <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> professor, by order of the Ministry of Magic, under the terms of <a href="/wiki/Educational_Decree_Number_Twenty-Two" title="Educational Decree Number Twenty-Two">Educational Decree Number Twenty-Two</a>, without Albus Dumbledore's consent. Her placement was to limit the learning of <a href="/wiki/Martial_magic" title="Martial magic">martial magic</a> and allow the Ministry to monitor the activities at Hogwarts.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> The Minister did this because of an unfounded fear that Dumbledore was trying to upturn his position as the Minister and was also afraid that Dumbledore was using the students as a means of overthrowing the Ministry.
</p><p>Moreover, Umbridge admitted that she was not fond of children, even expressing hatred for them, as she once confessed to Harry Potter.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTPF_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTPF-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> Having been denied any position of power and responsibility during her time as a student, Umbridge saw this return to school as a golden opportunity to wield power over those who had not (as she saw it) given her her due.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermoreprofile_1-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermoreprofile-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> During the Start-of Term Feast she gave a despairingly dull speech that <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> summed up as "<i>the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry</a> is interfering at Hogwarts</i>". The start of her speech began when she rudely interrupted Dumbledore with a cough, and she insulted the students by speaking to them condescendingly as though they were five-year old children. She essentially stated that progress in Defence Against the Dark Arts was going to be limited, but none of the students (aside from Hermione) were able to comprehend her dull speech and simply wandered off into their own discussions, while Umbridge ignorantly continued. Her rudeness and subliminal speech led many teachers to scorn her, as none except Dumbledore bowed back to her when she paused to bow at the staff. Upon finishing, she received very scattered and unenthusiastic applause, as most students lost track of her speech altogether, and the teachers barely clapped once or twice before stopping, showing their low regard for Umbridge. However, <a href="/wiki/Argus_Filch" title="Argus Filch">Argus Filch</a> was the one staff to genuinely applaud at the end.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/07/Umbridge_teaching.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160606154912" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="110" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Umbridge teaching.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge_teaching.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/07/Umbridge_teaching.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160606154912" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/07/Umbridge_teaching.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160606154912" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/07/Umbridge_teaching.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160606154912" decoding="async" width="250" height="110" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Umbridge teaching.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge_teaching.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/07/Umbridge_teaching.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160606154912" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Umbridge_teaching.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Umbridge teaching her DADA class purely defensive theory</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Well now, your teaching in this subject has been rather disrupted and fragmented, hasn’t it? The constant changing of teachers, many of whom do not seem to have followed any Ministry-approved curriculum, has unfortunately resulted in your being far below the standard we would expect to see in your O.W.L. year. You will be pleased to know, however, that these problems are now to be rectified. We will be following a carefully structured, theory-centred, Ministry-approved course of defensive magic this year. Copy down the following, please.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Umbridge justifying her biased and ineffective curriculum of her subject<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>She taught according to a politically restricted Ministry-approved curriculum. This curriculum entailed learning strictly the <a href="/wiki/Defensive_Magical_Theory" title="Defensive Magical Theory">theory of Defence Against the Dark Arts</a>, with no practical applications. Umbridge taught exclusively from a simplistic book: <i><a href="/wiki/Defensive_Magical_Theory" title="Defensive Magical Theory">Defensive Magical Theory</a></i>, by <a href="/wiki/Wilbert_Slinkhard" title="Wilbert Slinkhard">Wilbert Slinkhard</a>, which seemed, based on the chapter headings, to concern itself with negotiation and appeasement of, rather than actual defence against, the Dark Arts. By teaching basic defensive theory as opposed to real spells that would prepare her students for the outside world, she and the Ministry hoped to decrease the chance that Dumbledore could form a wizard army of students to overthrow the Ministry. Dolores proved to be ineffective as an educator. She had no teaching background and had trouble maintaining the class's attention. Because of these shortcomings she ordered her students to simply read from the book during class, denied them the rights to ask questions, and sat back behind her desk to simply observe.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/Dolores_Umbridge_In_Her_Office_Moment_WW.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200509174342" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dolores Umbridge In Her Office Moment WW.jpg" data-image-key="Dolores_Umbridge_In_Her_Office_Moment_WW.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/Dolores_Umbridge_In_Her_Office_Moment_WW.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200509174342" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/Dolores_Umbridge_In_Her_Office_Moment_WW.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200509174342" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/Dolores_Umbridge_In_Her_Office_Moment_WW.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200509174342" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dolores Umbridge In Her Office Moment WW.jpg" data-image-key="Dolores_Umbridge_In_Her_Office_Moment_WW.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/Dolores_Umbridge_In_Her_Office_Moment_WW.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200509174342" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dolores_Umbridge_In_Her_Office_Moment_WW.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Umbridge's pink and prim office as a professor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Most students were concerned and felt they would be left defenceless against the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a>, since the book was useless, and even if Voldemort was indeed dead and gone there were plenty of other dangerous things in the world to defend against. Some spoke out openly in class, such as: <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a>, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dean_Thomas" title="Dean Thomas">Dean Thomas</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Parvati_Patil" title="Parvati Patil">Parvati Patil</a>, but were immediately silenced or punished by Umbridge. Harry was the most outspoken, which often landed him in trouble.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>She steadfastly stuck to the Ministry line that <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> had not returned and that Harry Potter's claims were only to get attention for himself. When Harry dared to contradict the Ministry of Magic's stance, Umbridge punished him by giving him detention where he was forced to write the phrase "<i>I must not tell lies</i>" repeatedly with a <a href="/wiki/Black_Quill" title="Black Quill">Black Quill</a>; whatever the user wrote with it used their own blood as ink and sliced the words into their flesh, eventually leaving his hand permanently scarred. Owing to her lack of teaching ability, obvious disrespect towards the school and its residents and her unwavering loyalty to Fudge, Umbridge quickly became a heavily disliked person by the overwhelming majority of students and teachers alike.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="High_Inquisitor">High Inquisitor</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=8" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: High Inquisitor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: High Inquisitor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>An immediate success, totally revolutionising the teaching of Defence Against the Dark Arts and providing the Minister with on-the ground feedback about what’s really happening at Hogwarts.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/Percy_Weasley" title="Percy Weasley">Percy Weasley</a>'s biased and inaccurate regard of Dolores's teaching skills<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/Umbridge_inspecting_Flitwick.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180711114949" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Umbridge inspecting Flitwick.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge_inspecting_Flitwick.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/Umbridge_inspecting_Flitwick.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180711114949" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/Umbridge_inspecting_Flitwick.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180711114949" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/Umbridge_inspecting_Flitwick.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180711114949" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Umbridge inspecting Flitwick.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge_inspecting_Flitwick.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/Umbridge_inspecting_Flitwick.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180711114949" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Umbridge_inspecting_Flitwick.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Umbridge evaluating <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Filius Flitwick</a>, before measuring his height</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After working at Hogwarts for a short while and having a discussion with the Minister, <a href="/wiki/Educational_Decree_Number_Twenty-Three" title="Educational Decree Number Twenty-Three">Educational Decree Number Twenty-Three</a> increased Umbridge's power and influence in Hogwarts. She was appointed the first-ever "<a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_High_Inquisitor" title="Hogwarts High Inquisitor">Hogwarts High Inquisitor</a>" and used this position to evaluate, harass, and fire any teachers at Hogwarts deemed unsatisfactory by her or the Ministry. Umbridge was rude to many of the teachers she evaluated, especially those with close ties to <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Professor Dumbledore</a> and those she considered unfit to teach, such as <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Sybill Trelawney</a>. She even measured Flitwick's height with measuring tape. He was displeased and very offended by this disrespect. Some teachers refused to allow themselves to be intimidated, however; when inspecting Professor <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration_(class)" title="Transfiguration (class)">Transfiguration</a> class, Umbridge tried to harass Minerva with interruptions and false coughing, but Minerva either ignored them or retorted with scathing remarks.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8d/Umbridge_mcgonagall_controntation.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170817024243" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Umbridge mcgonagall controntation.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge_mcgonagall_controntation.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8d/Umbridge_mcgonagall_controntation.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170817024243" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8d/Umbridge_mcgonagall_controntation.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170817024243" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8d/Umbridge_mcgonagall_controntation.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170817024243" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Umbridge mcgonagall controntation.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge_mcgonagall_controntation.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8d/Umbridge_mcgonagall_controntation.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170817024243" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Umbridge_mcgonagall_controntation.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Umbridge exercises her power, creating and enforcing new school rules</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>To combat Umbridge's repressive stance of not teaching practical defensive magic, Harry formed a group to teach practical Defence Against the Dark Arts. However, Umbridge, learning that the group was created and afraid that the students would soon start to rebel against her, soon abolished all student groups of three or more members, meaning that students were not allowed to be seen together in a group whose members numbered three or more or they would be suspected of rule breaking. This also included <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> <a href="/wiki/Quidditch_team" title="Quidditch team">teams</a>. She permitted them to be reformed if they asked for permission, and only if she deemed them to be allowable, which meant that <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a> became an illegal organisation. The <a href="/wiki/Slytherin_Quidditch_team" title="Slytherin Quidditch team">Slytherin Quidditch team</a> was immediately given permission to reform, perhaps because Umbridge was from <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin House</a>, but she refused to allow the other teams permission under the excuse that she needed time to consider it. <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> at least had to wait an entire month before Professor McGonagall finally intervened and likely went to Professor Dumbledore to force it through.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p class="mw-empty-elt"></p><figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8f/Proclamation_-27_Poster.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20091129190520" class="image"><img alt="Proclamation -27 Poster.JPG" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="378" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Proclamation -27 Poster.JPG" data-image-key="Proclamation_-27_Poster.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8f/Proclamation_-27_Poster.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20091129190520" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8f/Proclamation_-27_Poster.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20091129190520" class="image"><img alt="Proclamation -27 Poster.JPG" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8f/Proclamation_-27_Poster.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20091129190520" decoding="async" width="250" height="378" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Proclamation -27 Poster.JPG" data-image-key="Proclamation_-27_Poster.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8f/Proclamation_-27_Poster.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20091129190520" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Proclamation_-27_Poster.JPG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p class="mw-empty-elt"></p><p>When Harry gave an interview about Voldemort to <i><a href="/wiki/The_Quibbler" title="The Quibbler">The Quibbler</a></i>, Umbridge then banned possession of the magazine to the point of risking expulsion from Hogwarts, and took away Harry's <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade" title="Hogsmeade">Hogsmeade</a> <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade_weekend_trips" title="Hogsmeade weekend trips">privileges</a> as a punishment for giving the interview, accusing him of giving false statements. However, by committing the former, Umbridge only caused the <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Streisand_effect" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Streisand effect">entire school to secretly read and discuss the Quibbler</a>.
</p><p>These actions were sanctioned by the <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Magic" title="Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> in the form of <a href="/wiki/Educational_Decree" title="Educational Decree">Educational Decrees</a>, but students merely found ways to circumvent or avoid them, often treating them as a joke. With her new authority, she attempted to dismiss <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Sybill Trelawney</a> as Professor of <a href="/wiki/Divination" title="Divination">Divination</a>; however, she was foiled in her attempt to send Trelawney away from the school, since Albus Dumbledore still had the power to keep Trelawney on school grounds and chose to exercise those powers.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Umbridge was horrified when Dumbledore replaced Trelawney with a <a href="/wiki/Centaur" title="Centaur">centaur</a> named <a href="/wiki/Firenze" title="Firenze">Firenze</a>; however, she could not prevent Firenze from being given the job, as the Ministry's rules only allowed her to appoint a new teacher <i>if</i> Dumbledore could not find one himself, since the Ministry was counting on Dumbledore being unable to find a new teacher. Umbridge considered Firenze, like all centaurs, as a "filthy half-breed".<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Headmistress">Headmistress</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=9" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Headmistress">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Headmistress"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>You filthy little beasts would never have dropped <a href="/wiki/Stink_Pellets" title="Stink Pellets">Stink Pellets</a> if you'd known I had it in my power to whip you raw, would you, now? Nobody would have thought of throwing <a href="/wiki/Fanged_Frisbee" title="Fanged Frisbee">Fanged Frisbees</a> down the corridors if I could've strung you up by the ankles in my office, would they? But when Educational Decree Number Twenty-Nine comes in...I'll be allowed to do them things...oh, things are going to be very different around here with </i>her<i> in charge! </i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/Argus_Filch" title="Argus Filch">Argus Filch</a> on Umbridge becoming Headmistress of Hogwarts<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/03/Kingsleywithfudge1.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20140922160847" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="127" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kingsleywithfudge1.JPG" data-image-key="Kingsleywithfudge1.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/03/Kingsleywithfudge1.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140922160847" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/03/Kingsleywithfudge1.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20140922160847" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/03/Kingsleywithfudge1.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140922160847" decoding="async" width="250" height="127" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kingsleywithfudge1.JPG" data-image-key="Kingsleywithfudge1.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/03/Kingsleywithfudge1.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140922160847" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kingsleywithfudge1.JPG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Umbridge and <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Fudge</a> confront Dumbledore about the D.A<a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">.</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, Umbridge and many other Slytherins found the <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">D.A.</a>'s headquarters in the <a href="/wiki/Room_of_Requirement" title="Room of Requirement">Room of Requirement</a>, after they were betrayed by <a href="/wiki/Marietta_Edgecombe" title="Marietta Edgecombe">Marietta Edgecombe</a>. Marietta betrayed the D.A. after Umbridge threatened to make sure her <a href="/wiki/Marietta_Edgecombe%27s_mother" class="mw-redirect" title="Marietta Edgecombe&#39;s mother">mother</a> would lose her job at the Ministry. She tried to prosecute Harry and have him thrown out of Hogwarts for forming the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> club, but <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a> took advantage of lack of evidence and the organisation's name to take the blame — claiming that he had invited the group to attend this meeting and no other such gatherings had taken place in the intervening time, and also the fact that the group was formed before it was made illegal — and he disappeared from Hogwarts, after a minor scuffle with <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Aurors</a> and the Minister for Magic himself. She soon after formed the <a href="/wiki/Inquisitorial_Squad" title="Inquisitorial Squad">Inquisitorial Squad</a>, made up entirely of <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherins</a>, which rewarded certain students for reporting on others and sanctioned them to act as enforcement goons.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d8/Dragon_firework_chasing_Umbridge.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140409230949" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="130" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dragon firework chasing Umbridge.gif" data-image-key="Dragon_firework_chasing_Umbridge.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d8/Dragon_firework_chasing_Umbridge.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140409230949" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d8/Dragon_firework_chasing_Umbridge.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140409230949" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d8/Dragon_firework_chasing_Umbridge.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140409230949" decoding="async" width="245" height="130" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dragon firework chasing Umbridge.gif" data-image-key="Dragon_firework_chasing_Umbridge.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d8/Dragon_firework_chasing_Umbridge.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140409230949" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dragon_firework_chasing_Umbridge.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Fred and <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George Weasley</a>'s fireworks terrify Umbridge</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Thanks to the newly passed <a href="/wiki/Educational_Decree_Number_Twenty-Eight" title="Educational Decree Number Twenty-Eight">Educational Decree Number Twenty-Eight</a>, Umbridge replaced Dumbledore as Headmistress. In response, the resentment simmering against her exploded into a full-fledged rebellion and Umbridge soon found herself on the receiving end of innumerable pranks, tricks and incidents designed to make her regret ever daring to set foot in Hogwarts. Many of these were orchestrated by <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred</a> and George Weasley, who led the resistance before Umbridge caught them, though they <a href="/wiki/Fred_and_George_Weasley%27s_departure_from_Hogwarts" title="Fred and George Weasley&#39;s departure from Hogwarts">flew away</a> on their brooms before she could have them whipped. Indeed, Hogwarts Castle itself seemed to join its inhabitants in making her life difficult, with <a href="/wiki/Peeves" title="Peeves">Peeves</a> the poltergeist (at Fred and George's request) spearheading the rebellion.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>This included doing things that made her work harder, like bursting out of blackboards, pushing over statues, toppling neatly stacked piles of parchment into fires, and following Umbridge around for hours, blowing raspberries every time she spoke. Umbridge had previously asked Cornelius Fudge to sign an order for the <a href="/wiki/Order_for_the_Expulsion_of_Peeves" title="Order for the Expulsion of Peeves">expulsion of Peeves</a>, but if any such order was ever signed, it was clearly unsuccessful at his removal, since it was impossible to kick him out of Hogwarts. Umbridge was also forced to rule as Headmistress from the Defence Against the Dark Arts Professor's <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts_Professor%27s_office" class="mw-redirect" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts Professor&#39;s office">office</a>, as the Headmaster's Tower refused to recognise her as the legitimate head of the school and sealed itself against her, causing her to throw a "right little tantrum".<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The teachers, who disliked Umbridge intensely, did as little as possible to help her in her duties, many going out of their way to make things more difficult for her by requesting her assistance in removing various charms and pranks by claiming that they weren't sure they had the 'authority' to do so. The teachers also lavished favours on Harry in the form of House Points and even sweets, specifically squeaking <a href="/wiki/Sugar_Mice" title="Sugar Mice">Sugar Mice</a> from <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Professor Flitwick</a>, for resisting against her.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP26_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP26-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/74/Fred_george_peeves.jpeg/revision/latest?cb=20180827191528" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="80" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Fred george peeves.jpeg" data-image-key="Fred_george_peeves.jpeg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/74/Fred_george_peeves.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20180827191528" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/74/Fred_george_peeves.jpeg/revision/latest?cb=20180827191528" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/74/Fred_george_peeves.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20180827191528" decoding="async" width="220" height="80" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Fred george peeves.jpeg" data-image-key="Fred_george_peeves.jpeg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/74/Fred_george_peeves.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20180827191528" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Fred_george_peeves.jpeg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Weasley twins tell Peeves to "give her hell from us"</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Minerva McGonagall, who normally intensely disliked Peeves and his antics, refused to stop him and even gave him advice on how to perform his actions. The only staff member who supported Umbridge whole-heartedly was the caretaker, <a href="/wiki/Argus_Filch" title="Argus Filch">Argus Filch</a>, who grew to like her methods, as well as being given permission to torture students himself. She later fired Gamekeeper <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a>, as he was a <a href="/wiki/Half-giant" title="Half-giant">half-giant</a>. When attempting to subdue and force Hagrid off the school's grounds with five Ministry of Magic officials, they seriously injured Professor <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>, who was protesting the force used to wrangle Hagrid, which was so scandalous that, while the event was occurring, an O.W.L. Astronomy test was just near the action and even the instructor objected.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Umbridge worked hard to intercept and monitor all means of communication. She tried to prevent Harry Potter from contacting his godfather <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>. She read all incoming and outgoing student mail, and even <a href="/wiki/Hedwig" title="Hedwig">Hedwig</a>, Harry Potter's owl, was injured. Even though it was hypothetically suggested that Hedwig was attacked by a <a href="/wiki/Thestral" title="Thestral">Thestral</a> by <a href="/wiki/Wilhelmina_Grubbly-Plank" title="Wilhelmina Grubbly-Plank">Professor Grubbly-Plank</a>, a more likely possibility was that Hedwig was injured by Umbridge in an attempt to obtain the letter she carried from Sirius Black.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP17_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP17-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Skirmish_in_the_Forbidden_Forest">Skirmish in the Forbidden Forest</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=10" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Skirmish in the Forbidden Forest">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Skirmish in the Forbidden Forest"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Skirmish_in_the_Forbidden_Forest" title="Skirmish in the Forbidden Forest">Skirmish in the Forbidden Forest</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Umbridge</b>: "<i>Of course. Of course... very well, then... you two stay ahead of me.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>Can we have your wand, then, if we're going first?</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Umbridge</b>: "<i>No, I don't think so, Mr Potter. The Ministry places a rather higher value on my life than yours, I’m afraid.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Harry and Hermione leading Umbridge into the forest<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180203175328" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="116" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933.jpg" data-image-key="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180203175328" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180203175328" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180203175328" decoding="async" width="250" height="116" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933.jpg" data-image-key="Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180203175328" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Order-of-the-phoenix-movie-screencaps.com-11933.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Umbridge asking Snape for <a href="/wiki/Veritaserum" title="Veritaserum">Veritaserum</a> in order to interrogate Harry</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Soon afterwards, Umbridge caught Harry trying to use the <a href="/wiki/Floo_Network" title="Floo Network">Floo Network</a> in her office while trying to contact Sirius, and he and his friends and fellow D.A. members <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a>, <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a> were held in her office by Inquisitorial Squad members. When Harry refused to tell her what he had been doing, Umbridge first attempted to dose him with <a href="/wiki/Veritaserum" title="Veritaserum">Veritaserum</a>, but <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Professor Snape</a> told her he had no more, as she had squandered it all when interrogating students. She did this on account of not knowing the proper amount to give the students.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Nooooo! Noooooo... I am Senior Undersecretary... you cannot... unhand me, you animals... nooooo!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Umbridge being dragged away by Centaurs<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Centaurs_Take_Dolores_OotP.png/revision/latest?cb=20170106070600" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Centaurs Take Dolores OotP.png" data-image-key="Centaurs_Take_Dolores_OotP.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Centaurs_Take_Dolores_OotP.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170106070600" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Centaurs_Take_Dolores_OotP.png/revision/latest?cb=20170106070600" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Centaurs_Take_Dolores_OotP.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170106070600" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Centaurs Take Dolores OotP.png" data-image-key="Centaurs_Take_Dolores_OotP.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3c/Centaurs_Take_Dolores_OotP.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170106070600" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Centaurs_Take_Dolores_OotP.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Centaurs drag Dolores Umbridge away upon being called 'filthy <a href="/wiki/Half-breed" title="Half-breed">half-breeds</a>' and 'creatures of near-human intelligence'</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>She then claimed that the illegal <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a> might "<i>loosen his tongue</i>". Hermione, much in shock, protested against it, but Umbridge simply brushed her off and noted that what "Cornelius doesn't know, cannot hurt him." She also revealed that she had made the order to release dementors on Harry and his cousin Dudley, believing that it was the most effective way to silence what she believed to be false claims about <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>'s return.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> Desperate, Hermione tricked Umbridge into following her and Harry into the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a> in search of an alleged "secret weapon" of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>. There, Umbridge was confronted by a herd of <a href="/wiki/Centaur" title="Centaur">centaurs</a>, whom she shamelessly insulted with racial slurs and arrogance. Umbridge then attacked one of the centaurs near her, and as a result, she was chased and nearly killed by them. Although she survived, her <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge%27s_wand" title="Dolores Umbridge&#39;s wand">wand</a> was snapped in half when one of the centaurs stepped on it.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Umbridge was ultimately rescued by Dumbledore, although she was apparently left with a significant fear of centaurs afterwards, reacting violently at even the sound of hoofbeats. How Dumbledore managed to rescue her from the human-hating centaurs without suffering any injury himself remained a mystery, though it is likely that the centaurs in the Forbidden Forest had respect for Albus, based on their salute at his funeral.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Suspension">Suspension</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=11" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Suspension">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Suspension"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 213px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Umbridge_suspended.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180220025719" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="211" height="201" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Umbridge suspended.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge_suspended.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Umbridge_suspended.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/211?cb=20180220025719" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Umbridge_suspended.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180220025719" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Umbridge_suspended.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/211?cb=20180220025719" decoding="async" width="211" height="201" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Umbridge suspended.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge_suspended.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Umbridge_suspended.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/211?cb=20180220025719" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Umbridge_suspended.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The <i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Prophet" title="Daily Prophet">Daily Prophet</a></i> announces Umbridge's suspension after the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After Voldemort appeared in the Ministry of Magic and was seen by a number of people, including <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a>, Dumbledore was restored as the Headmaster and Umbridge was suspended following allegations of abuse. Umbridge, who had been in the school's hospital wing, attempted to sneak out of the castle on the second-to-last day of term during the evening meal. But fate had her run right into <a href="/wiki/Peeves" title="Peeves">Peeves</a> the <a href="/wiki/Poltergeist" title="Poltergeist">poltergeist</a>, who took advantage of his final opportunity to fulfil the request of Fred and George and chased her gleefully from the premises.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Peeves did this while beating her over the head alternately with a walking stick and a sock full of <a href="/wiki/Chalk" title="Chalk">chalk</a>, leading a crowd of delighted students whose teachers made only a few feeble attempts to restrain them. Professor <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a> expressed regret at not being able to chase Umbridge herself, because Peeves had borrowed her walking stick and she was not fully recovered.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/B5C30_Peeves_chasing_Umbridge.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161218171626" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="129" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B5C30 Peeves chasing Umbridge.jpg" data-image-key="B5C30_Peeves_chasing_Umbridge.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/B5C30_Peeves_chasing_Umbridge.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161218171626" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/B5C30_Peeves_chasing_Umbridge.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161218171626" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/B5C30_Peeves_chasing_Umbridge.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161218171626" decoding="async" width="250" height="129" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B5C30 Peeves chasing Umbridge.jpg" data-image-key="B5C30_Peeves_chasing_Umbridge.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/B5C30_Peeves_chasing_Umbridge.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161218171626" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B5C30_Peeves_chasing_Umbridge.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Peeves chasing Umbridge with McGonagall's cane</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Return_to_the_Ministry">Return to the Ministry</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=12" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Return to the Ministry">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Return to the Ministry"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Despite all of her actions at Hogwarts, Umbridge later returned to the position of Senior Under-Secretary at the Ministry and told the new Minister, <a href="/wiki/Rufus_Scrimgeour" title="Rufus Scrimgeour">Rufus Scrimgeour</a>, about Harry's wish to become an Auror, to Harry's anger. In fact, one of the reasons why Harry refused to trust the <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Magic" title="Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> and Scrimgeour was that Umbridge was never sacked and arrested for her actions at Hogwarts. She was later seen at <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>'s funeral at Hogwarts, though she did not speak and was startled by the sight of <a href="/wiki/Firenze" title="Firenze">Firenze</a>. She feigned grief and looked scandalised when Hagrid blew his nose with loud trumpeting noises.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP30_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP30-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Muggle-Born_Registration_Commission">Muggle-Born Registration Commission</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=13" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Muggle-Born Registration Commission">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Muggle-Born Registration Commission"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Alderton</b>: "<i>No, no, I'm half-blood, I tell you! My father was a wizard, he was, look him up, Arkie Alderton, he's a well known broomstick designer, look him up, I tell you — get your hands off me, get your hands off —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Umbridge</b>: "<i>This is your final warning. If you struggle, you will be subjected to the <a href="/wiki/Dementor%27s_Kiss" title="Dementor&#39;s Kiss">Dementor's Kiss</a>. Take him away.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Umbridge overseeing a biased trial<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
