<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/91/Thicknesse_regime.png/revision/latest?cb=20170103025010" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="188" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Thicknesse regime.png" data-image-key="Thicknesse_regime.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/91/Thicknesse_regime.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170103025010" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/91/Thicknesse_regime.png/revision/latest?cb=20170103025010" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/91/Thicknesse_regime.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170103025010" decoding="async" width="250" height="188" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Thicknesse regime.png" data-image-key="Thicknesse_regime.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/91/Thicknesse_regime.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170103025010" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Thicknesse_regime.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Four of the most consequential figures of the new regime (left to right): <a href="/wiki/Albert_Runcorn" title="Albert Runcorn">Albert Runcorn</a>, Ministry Official; Dolores Umbridge, <a href="/wiki/Senior_Undersecretary_to_the_Minister_for_Magic" title="Senior Undersecretary to the Minister for Magic">Senior Undersecretary to the Minister</a> and Head of the Muggle-Born Registration Commission; <a href="/wiki/Pius_Thicknesse" title="Pius Thicknesse">Pius Thicknesse</a>, <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Magic" title="Minister for Magic">Minister for Magic</a>; and <a href="/wiki/Corban_Yaxley" title="Corban Yaxley">Corban Yaxley</a>, Head of the <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Magical_Law_Enforcement" title="Department of Magical Law Enforcement">Department of Magical Law Enforcement</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Following Lord Voldemort's takeover of the <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Magic" title="Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, Umbridge resumed her post as Under-Secretary and oversaw the registration and persecution of <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-born</a> witches and wizards under the <a href="/wiki/Muggle-Born_Registration_Commission" title="Muggle-Born Registration Commission">Muggle-Born Registration Commission</a>. She conducted trials subjecting innocent Muggle-borns to the presence of <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a> and sending them to <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> for supposedly stealing magic from "real" witches and wizards. She also wrote the propaganda booklet <i><a href="/wiki/Mudbloods_and_the_Dangers_They_Pose_to_a_Peaceful_Pure-Blood_Society" title="Mudbloods and the Dangers They Pose to a Peaceful Pure-Blood Society">Mudbloods and the Dangers They Pose to a Peaceful Pure-Blood Society</a></i>, which featured a cover including a <a href="/wiki/Rose" title="Rose">rose</a> being strangled by green weeds.<sup id="cite_ref-DH13_5-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH13-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Following <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a>'s murder at the hands of <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a>, Umbridge somehow took possession of his <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody%27s_magical_eye" title="Alastor Moody&#39;s magical eye">magical eye</a>. Affixing it to her office door, she could terrorise all Ministry employees with the mere concept that she could observe their every move.<sup id="cite_ref-DH13_5-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH13-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/36/Mugglebornregistration.png/revision/latest?cb=20110823192534" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="105" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Mugglebornregistration.png" data-image-key="Mugglebornregistration.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/36/Mugglebornregistration.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110823192534" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/36/Mugglebornregistration.png/revision/latest?cb=20110823192534" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/36/Mugglebornregistration.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110823192534" decoding="async" width="250" height="105" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Mugglebornregistration.png" data-image-key="Mugglebornregistration.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/36/Mugglebornregistration.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110823192534" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Mugglebornregistration.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dolores overseeing <a href="/wiki/Mary_Cattermole" title="Mary Cattermole">Mary Cattermole</a>'s trial before the Muggle-Born Registration Commission</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>At some point, Umbridge received a locket as a bribe from petty thief <a href="/wiki/Mundungus_Fletcher" title="Mundungus Fletcher">Mundungus Fletcher</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH11_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH11-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> This locket was <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Locket" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Locket">Salazar Slytherin's Locket</a>, which had once been owned by <a href="/wiki/Merope_Riddle" title="Merope Riddle">Merope Gaunt</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hepzibah_Smith" title="Hepzibah Smith">Hepzibah Smith</a>. Umbridge was unaware that the locket was one of Lord Voldemort's <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a> (or belonged to him at all), but she chose to lie about the meaning of the <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/cloisonn%C3%A9" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:cloisonné">cloisonné</a> <i>S</i>, stating it was a <a href="/wiki/Selwyn_family" title="Selwyn family">Selwyn family</a> heirloom, a name which she believed would bolster her pure-blood credentials (the family has dark connections; a Death Eater who responds to <a href="/wiki/Xenophilius_Lovegood" title="Xenophilius Lovegood">Xenophilius Lovegood</a> was named thus, meaning that Dolores chose the name as it commanded a degree of respect among the supporters of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>'s regime).<sup id="cite_ref-DH13_5-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH13-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/73/DH1_Harry_as_Albert_Runcorn_stunning_Umbridge.gif/revision/latest?cb=20180827041418" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="103" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DH1 Harry as Albert Runcorn stunning Umbridge.gif" data-image-key="DH1_Harry_as_Albert_Runcorn_stunning_Umbridge.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/73/DH1_Harry_as_Albert_Runcorn_stunning_Umbridge.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20180827041418" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/73/DH1_Harry_as_Albert_Runcorn_stunning_Umbridge.gif/revision/latest?cb=20180827041418" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/73/DH1_Harry_as_Albert_Runcorn_stunning_Umbridge.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20180827041418" decoding="async" width="245" height="103" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DH1 Harry as Albert Runcorn stunning Umbridge.gif" data-image-key="DH1_Harry_as_Albert_Runcorn_stunning_Umbridge.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/73/DH1_Harry_as_Albert_Runcorn_stunning_Umbridge.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20180827041418" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DH1_Harry_as_Albert_Runcorn_stunning_Umbridge.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dolores and <a href="/wiki/Corban_Yaxley" title="Corban Yaxley">Yaxley</a> being stunned</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Umbridge</b>: "<i>A wand was taken from you upon your arrival at the Ministry today, Mrs Cattermole. Eight-and-three quarter inches, <a href="/wiki/Cherry_(tree)" title="Cherry (tree)">cherry</a>, <a href="/wiki/Unicorn_hair" title="Unicorn hair">unicorn-hair</a> <a href="/wiki/Wand_core" title="Wand core">core</a>. Do you recognise that description?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Marry Cattermole</b>: "<i>T-took? I didn’t t-take it from anybody. I b-bought it when I was eleven years old. It — it — it — chose me.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Umbridge</b>: "<i>No,no, I don’t think so, Mrs Cattermole. Wands only choose witches or wizards. You are not a witch. I have your responses to the questionnaire that was sent to you here — Mafalda, pass them to me.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Umbridge's cruel and arbitary trial for Marry Cattermole, showing her hatred and prejudice towards Muggle-borns<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>She boasted of this supposed connection to <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, who was in the guise of Ministry employee <a href="/wiki/Mafalda_Hopkirk" title="Mafalda Hopkirk">Mafalda Hopkirk</a>, during one of Umbridge's <a href="/wiki/Blood_status" title="Blood status">blood purity</a> hearings, of the <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-born</a> witch <a href="/wiki/Mary_Cattermole" title="Mary Cattermole">Mary Cattermole</a>. During the meeting, she admonished Cattermole for having greengrocer Muggle parents and interrogated her regarding her <a href="/wiki/Mary_Cattermole%27s_wand" title="Mary Cattermole&#39;s wand">wand</a>, falsely claiming that she stole it. She also used her <a href="/wiki/Persian_cat" title="Persian cat">persian cat</a> <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a> to keep the <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementor</a> guards at bay. At that moment after she incredulously lied about her blood status and derided Cattermole, Harry Potter, who was full of rage under his <a href="/wiki/Cloak_of_Invisibility" title="Cloak of Invisibility">Cloak of Invisibility</a>, attacked Umbridge and <a href="/wiki/Corban_Yaxley" title="Corban Yaxley">Yaxley</a> with the <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">Stunning Spell</a>. Umbridge was stunned, leaving Harry and Hermione free to snatch the locket from around Umbridge's neck and flee the scene. Hermione then <a href="/wiki/Doubling_Charm" title="Doubling Charm">created a copy</a> of the locket to leave with Umbridge, so that she did not become suspicious.<sup id="cite_ref-DH13_5-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH13-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Hermione (as Malfalda)</b>: "<i>That’s — that’s pretty, Dolores</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Dolores</b>: "<i>What? Oh yes — an old family heirloom, The S stands for Selwyn. . . . I am related to the Selwyns. . . . Indeed, there are few pure-blood families to whom I am not related.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Umbridge lying about her blood status<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>Most likely due to her mother being a Muggle and father being a source of embarrassment, Umbridge used the locket to emphasise her wizarding ancestry, to make herself seem more appealing to the new regime by distracting attention from her <a href="/wiki/Muggle" class="mw-redirect" title="Muggle">non-wizarding</a> ancestors. When the locket was in the possession of Harry Potter and companions, it exerted a malign influence on each of them when they wore it. Due to Umbridge's wicked nature, she had unknowingly enjoyed an "affinity" with the object and so the Horcrux — rather than impart a negative effect on her — <i>strengthened</i> her.<sup id="cite_ref-online_bloomsbury_chat_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-online_bloomsbury_chat-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> Umbridge presumably continued prosecuting Muggle-Borns throughout the next year.
</p>
<h3><span id="Imprisonment_(1998)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Imprisonment_.281998.29">Imprisonment <span class="template-c">(1998)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=14" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Imprisonment (1998)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Imprisonment (1998)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f0/Daily_Prophet-foundable_1.png/revision/latest?cb=20200817063204" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="180" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Daily Prophet-foundable 1.png" data-image-key="Daily_Prophet-foundable_1.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f0/Daily_Prophet-foundable_1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200817063204" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f0/Daily_Prophet-foundable_1.png/revision/latest?cb=20200817063204" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f0/Daily_Prophet-foundable_1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200817063204" decoding="async" width="180" height="180" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Daily Prophet-foundable 1.png" data-image-key="Daily_Prophet-foundable_1.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f0/Daily_Prophet-foundable_1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200817063204" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Daily_Prophet-foundable_1.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The <i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Prophet" title="Daily Prophet">Daily Prophet</a></i> announces Umbridge's imprisonment in <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After Lord Voldemort's death at Harry Potter's hands and the reformation of the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> by <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Shacklebolt" title="Kingsley Shacklebolt">Kingsley Shacklebolt</a>, Umbridge was arrested, tried, convicted and sent to <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> for life for her crimes against Muggle-borns, as not all of them survived.<sup id="cite_ref-imprisonment_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-imprisonment-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_timeline">Alternative timeline</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=15" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Alternative timeline">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Alternative timeline"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Cursed Child"><b>Dolores Umbridge</b>: "<i>Scorpius Malfoy. Get out of the lake. Get out of the lake. Right now.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Scorpius Malfoy</b>: "<i>Miss. I need help. Please, Miss.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Dolores Umbridge</b>: "<i>Miss? I'm Professor Umbridge, the headmistress of your school, I'm no Miss.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Scorpius after arriving into an alternate timeline<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Cursed_Child" title="Harry Potter and the Cursed Child">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>23 years after the Battle of Hogwarts, when <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Potter</a> and <a href="/wiki/Scorpius_Malfoy" title="Scorpius Malfoy">Scorpius Malfoy</a> time-travelled to the Second Task in the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a> in order to save <a href="/wiki/Cedric_Diggory" title="Cedric Diggory">Cedric</a>, they created an alternative world in which Voldemort won in the Battle of Hogwarts. In this world, Umbridge was the Headmistress of Hogwarts. When Scorpius Malfoy emerged from the <a href="/wiki/Great_Lake" title="Great Lake">Great Lake</a>, he was discovered by Umbridge, whom he questioned about Albus Potter. Umbridge was surprised at the question informs him that there has been no Potter at Hogwarts since Harry was killed at The Battle of Hogwarts, much to Scorpius' shock. Dementors then descended upon the two as Umbridge told Scorpius that he was upsetting the Dementors and spoiling "Voldemort Day".<sup id="cite_ref-CC_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CC-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>A few days later, Umbridge called Scorpius to her office to discuss his newfound obsession with Harry Potter's death and Cedric Diggory, but Scorpius managed to fool her and subvert her suspicions. She then dismissed him to go to his next class. Later that night after Ron and Hermione had been killed by Dementors, Umbridge discovered Snape and Scorpius down by the lake. When she demanded to know about Snape's treachery, the latter asked her how long she has known about his true loyalty, to which Umbridge replied she had known for years and regretted not acting upon her suspicions. As she was about to attack the two, Snape used the <a href="/wiki/Banishing_Charm" title="Banishing Charm">Banishing Charm</a> to send Umbridge flying backwards, buying Scorpius enough time to escape into the lake before the Dementors <a href="/wiki/Dementor%27s_Kiss" title="Dementor&#39;s Kiss">consumed his soul</a> to restore the timeline.<sup id="cite_ref-CC_22-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CC-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_appearance">Physical appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=16" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Physical appearance">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Physical appearance"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Pottermore">"<i>Dolores Umbridge is said to resemble a ‘large, pale toad’.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Physical description<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Pottermore" title="Pottermore">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5a/Dolores_Umbridge.PNG/revision/latest?cb=20150825230359" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="330" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dolores Umbridge.PNG" data-image-key="Dolores_Umbridge.PNG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5a/Dolores_Umbridge.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20150825230359" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5a/Dolores_Umbridge.PNG/revision/latest?cb=20150825230359" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5a/Dolores_Umbridge.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20150825230359" decoding="async" width="220" height="330" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dolores Umbridge.PNG" data-image-key="Dolores_Umbridge.PNG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5a/Dolores_Umbridge.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20150825230359" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dolores_Umbridge.PNG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dolores Umbridge</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Dolores Umbridge was described to be a short squat woman resembling a large pale toad. She had a broad, flabby face, a wide, slack mouth, and little neck. Her eyes were bulging and pouchy, and in her mousy brown hair she often wore a black velvet bow, which reminded Harry of a fly perched dangerously above a <a href="/wiki/Toad" title="Toad">toad</a>, furthering Umbridge's toad-like characteristics. She spoke with a simpering high-pitched voice that was girlish and breathless, contrary to her appearance (Harry expected a croak) and decorated her office with kittens and other cute pink paraphernalia. Her wide toad-like smile and tendency to speak in a sugary voice that was often described as poisoned honey was a physical exemplification of her cruelty that was barely hidden by her seemingly harmless dress-style. Umbridge's thick stubby fingers were adorned with several gaudy old rings.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> She also was said to have a big chest, as noted by Harry Potter when he saw Slytherin's locket lying there.<sup id="cite_ref-DH13_5-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH13-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Umbridge was seen wearing various green tweed outfits, usually with a pink fuzzy cardigan on top, giving her greater toad-like qualities. The head-to-toe matching outfits, usually in shades of pink, were worn while she taught and during her duties as High Inquisitor. According to Harry, she looked like someone's maiden aunt, and that her style of dressing would fit someone half her age. During <a href="/wiki/Disciplinary_hearing_of_Harry_Potter" title="Disciplinary hearing of Harry Potter">Harry's hearing regarding under-age magic</a>, Umbridge wore the black robes of the <a href="/wiki/Wizengamot" title="Wizengamot">Wizengamot</a> with a silver "W" on it.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Also, while she interrogated Muggle-borns, she wore <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_locket" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s locket">Salazar Slytherin's locket</a> on top of her frilly girlish pink outfits in an attempt to prove her <a href="/wiki/Blood_status" title="Blood status">blood purity</a>, claiming that the S stood for the pure-blood <a href="/wiki/Selwyn_family" title="Selwyn family">Selwyn family</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH13_5-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH13-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> However, since her imprisonment in Azkaban, it is unlikely that she wore any of her old outfits, but instead wore the black and white striped uniform of all prisoners.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality_and_traits">Personality and traits</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=17" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Personality and traits">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Personality and traits"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Sirius Black</b>: "<i>I know [Umbridge] by reputation and I'm sure she's no Death Eater —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>She's foul enough to be one...</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Harry telling <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> his views on Umbridge<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>Dolores Umbridge was an evil woman, who represented the very worst of political power. She was extremely ruthless, cruel, callous, brutal, corrupt, sadistic, arrogant, intolerant, power-hungry and devoid of any kind of moral or ethical centre. She was apathetic and absolutist, yet also a committed and flexible witch who was dogmatically supportive of the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">British Ministry of Magic</a>, eagerly obeying the every command of <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rufus_Scrimgeour" title="Rufus Scrimgeour">Rufus Scrimgeour</a> and <a href="/wiki/Pius_Thicknesse" title="Pius Thicknesse">Pius Thicknesse</a> when in their respective terms of power, in order to gain power herself. She was even willing to go to Hogwarts for Fudge, in spite of her bad memories there and strong dislike of children. She was depicted using any means to maintain the political power of her bosses, often flaunting the power she in turn obtained during her time in Hogwarts. She committed attempted soul-removal (via the Dementor attack on Harry), solicited bribes, and tortured children to achieve her goals. Her draconian ideals of discipline, such as having victims write lines in their own blood using a <a href="/wiki/Black_Quill" title="Black Quill">Black Quill</a>, which carves the words into the back of the writer's hand, were considered by Harry and Ron to be "sick".<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Although Umbridge saw such deeds as doing what was necessary, they ultimately amounted to a form of "the ends justify the means".
</p><p>Her fanatical loyalty clouded her judgement and caused her to place a blind faith in authority, believing that it could not possibly be wrong, and even after it was proven wrong she did not change her opinion, as was clearly seen when she was loyal to Fudge over Dumbledore, rather than accepting the truth, and then abandoning Fudge when he was ousted from his office. However, as he was out of the picture, she was flexible enough to turn her loyalty towards Scrimgeour, proving she was more loyal to the cause than its leader and therefore continued to show the authorities her unbreakable devotion. However, when Fudge gave her power, it inflated her sense of self-importance and instilled a sense of ruthlessness, making her seek to exercise complete control over everyone and everything around her.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Even as a student, she was resentful that the school did not grant her any position of power and responsibility, and felt that she was deprived of a chance to exercise authority over her peers.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermoreprofile_1-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermoreprofile-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Umbridge's strictness bordered on the ideal representation of the qualities of a totalitarian government. From her perspective, free speech, dissent, diversity and multiple points of view could not be tolerated. She led not by consensus and respect, but rather by fear and intimidation; as the year progressed, she grew more independent of Fudge's will by beginning to use her own available resources in order to make people obey her, even attempting to use the restricted <a href="/wiki/Veritaserum" title="Veritaserum">Veritaserum</a> and then the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a> on <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> when he would not give her desired information.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Umbridge was capable and intelligent, as she was high-ranking in the Ministry at a relatively young age, although her general magical knowledge seemed limited. She unreasonably demanded Snape to brew <a href="/wiki/Veritaserum" title="Veritaserum">Veritaserum</a> in less than the required month after she squandered an entire bottle on one previous interrogation, although Snape had told her that three drops would suffice. She also could not figure out how the students were suffering from the symptoms of "<a href="/wiki/Umbridge-itis" title="Umbridge-itis">Umbridge-itis</a>," nor how to remove the <a href="/wiki/Weasleys%27_Wildfire_Whiz-bangs" title="Weasleys&#39; Wildfire Whiz-bangs">Weasleys' Wildfire Whiz-bangs</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Portable_Swamp" title="Portable Swamp">Portable Swamp</a> left by <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred</a> and <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George Weasley</a>, which Flitwick vanished in a matter of seconds.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/OOTP_HQ_still_Umbridge_in_her_Hogwarts_office.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160721183557" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="207" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="OOTP HQ still Umbridge in her Hogwarts office.jpg" data-image-key="OOTP_HQ_still_Umbridge_in_her_Hogwarts_office.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/OOTP_HQ_still_Umbridge_in_her_Hogwarts_office.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160721183557" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/OOTP_HQ_still_Umbridge_in_her_Hogwarts_office.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160721183557" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/OOTP_HQ_still_Umbridge_in_her_Hogwarts_office.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160721183557" decoding="async" width="250" height="207" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="OOTP HQ still Umbridge in her Hogwarts office.jpg" data-image-key="OOTP_HQ_still_Umbridge_in_her_Hogwarts_office.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/OOTP_HQ_still_Umbridge_in_her_Hogwarts_office.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160721183557" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:OOTP_HQ_still_Umbridge_in_her_Hogwarts_office.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dolores Umbridge at her desk with her kitten plates</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Her cruelty was disguised by her quiet, childish, high-pitched voice (which both took Harry aback and made the hair on his neck stand up straight, as he had childishly expected a croak), as well by decorating her office with paraphernalia related to <a href="/wiki/Cat" title="Cat">kittens</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chocolate_cake" title="Chocolate cake">chocolate cakes</a>, <a href="/wiki/Biscuit" title="Biscuit">biscuits</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tea" title="Tea">tea</a>, and other cute things to the point of coming across as sickening to her enemies despite her genuine appreciation for them.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Although she liked kittens (hence her decorations relating to them), she doubted she was responsible enough to actually care for real ones, and so maintained her focus on decorations.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermoreprofile_1-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermoreprofile-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> Her personality has been described as "<a href="/wiki/Poison" title="Poison">poisoned</a> <a href="/wiki/Honey" title="Honey">honey</a>," and it was said on various occasions that the sweeter her voice was, the more dangerous or infuriated she became.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>She also tended to give her signature fake cough, "<i>Hem-Hem</i>," when she wanted someone's attention, rudely interrupting them, as well as usually speaking to people she felt were beneath her in a very condescending tone, as if they were simpletons or very young children, both of which she hated.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Umbridge expressing contempt towards &#91;&#91;Centaur&#93;&#93;s"><b>Bane</b>: "<i>I asked you who are you, human.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Dolores Umbridge</b>: "<i>I am Dolores Umbridge! Senior Undersecretary to the Minister of Magic and Headmistress and High Inquisitor of Hogwarts!</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Magorian</b>: "<i>You are from the Ministry of Magic?</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Dolores Umbridge</b>: "<i>That's right! So be very careful! By the laws laid down by the <a href="/wiki/Department_for_the_Regulation_and_Control_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Department for the Regulation and Control of Magical Creatures">Department for the Regulation and Control of Magical Creatures</a>, any attack by half-breeds such as yourselves on a human —</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Umbridge expressing contempt towards <a href="/wiki/Centaur" title="Centaur">Centaurs</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>For unknown reasons, but most likely because of the Ministry's beliefs, Umbridge was fanatically prejudiced against part-humans (such as werewolves and half-giants), which she called "<a href="/wiki/Half-breeds" class="mw-redirect" title="Half-breeds">half-breeds</a>". It was her prejudice that caused her to pass a series of anti-<a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolf</a> legislation, which made it almost illegal for those afflicted with <a href="/wiki/Lycanthropy" title="Lycanthropy">lycanthropy</a> to hold jobs. Her prejudice also led to her mistakenly believe that mermaids and centaurs were part-humans, when in fact they were separate species, and in her haste of prosecuting them she would forgo her usual feigned politeness, and be outright rude. However, after the incident with the Hogwarts centaurs, she developed a phobia of centaurs. An odd derivative from this prejudice was that, despite her hatred of half-breeds, Umbridge did not seem to hate <a href="/wiki/Half-goblin" title="Half-goblin">part-goblin</a> <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Filius Flitwick</a> (most likely due to lack of knowledge of Flitwick's ancestry and his undeniably skilled teaching methods), as <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred Weasley</a> stated that she marked him well on his inspection.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Umbridge was a <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood_supremacy" title="Pure-blood supremacy">pure-blood supremacist</a>, stemming from her childhood when her brother was discovered to be a Squib. Hating her mother for being a Muggle, Dolores would blame her for being the cause of her brother's lack of magical powers. After bribing her father to quietly leave public sight, Dolores lied to everyone that she was a pure-blood, believing it would give her social respect and status, later bolstering her credentials by falsely claiming that she was related to the <a href="/wiki/Selwyn_family" title="Selwyn family">Selwyn family</a> (albeit controlled by Voldemort's <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a> <a href="/wiki/Slytherin%27s_Locket" title="Slytherin&#39;s Locket">locket</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-pottermoreprofile_1-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermoreprofile-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> She was known to spout very uncharitable views on the non-magical community when intoxicated, to the point that even fellow pro-pure-blood coworkers were shocked by her. While sober, Dolores would put up a facade of politeness for Muggle-borns, repressing her prejudice for them to maintain her public image; only when Voldemort took over the Ministry did she unleash her cruelty over them, tormenting them with sham trials and sadistically sending them off to Azkaban.<sup id="cite_ref-DH13_5-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH13-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Her lust for power and social status turned her against her own family, though it is unknown how they treated her. Despising her Muggle mother and Squib brother as second class citizens while ashamed of her lowly janitorial employee of a father, Dolores would never speak of any of them again while shunning her father with a bribe, and went onto inventing her ancestry to make herself seem more noble to the higher ups. Dolores also attempted to seduce her superiors into marriage, not out of <a href="/wiki/Love" title="Love">love</a>, but for the social elevation and security it would provide, though she was always turned down as her obsession turned off any co-workers she flirted with. Her power-hungry nature was evident even as a child, as she came to despise her time as a student at Hogwarts because she was not given any power of authority, and upon returning as a Ministry-implanted teacher, she saw it as an opportunity to get what she thought was wrongly denied in her youth, heavily flaunting all the titles and power that Fudge granted her.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermoreprofile_1-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermoreprofile-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ea/Umbridge_mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170817024425" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Umbridge mcgonagall.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge_mcgonagall.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ea/Umbridge_mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170817024425" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ea/Umbridge_mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170817024425" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ea/Umbridge_mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170817024425" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Umbridge mcgonagall.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge_mcgonagall.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ea/Umbridge_mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170817024425" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Umbridge_mcgonagall.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Umbridge trying to exert her power over McGonagall</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Umbridge was known to rapidly resort to cruel and unusual punishments over perceived slights and take great pleasure in such punishments. Umbridge also liked to showcase her statuses, as she arrogantly told the centaurs in the Forbidden Forest of her many titles, and mounted plaques on her office doors to display these titles. Unaware that she was in possession of <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Locket" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Locket">Salazar Slytherin's Locket</a>, she falsely claimed it was a family heirloom and proof of her relation to the <a href="/wiki/Selwyn_family" title="Selwyn family">Selwyn family</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH13_5-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH13-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite her confidence bordering on arrogance, Umbridge knew she could not do Cornelius Fudge's will at Hogwarts without help, and so enlisted <a href="/wiki/Argus_Filch" title="Argus Filch">Argus Filch</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Inquisitorial_Squad" title="Inquisitorial Squad">Inquisitorial Squad</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Umbridge</b>: "<i> No, not with your quill, you’re going to be using a rather special one of mine. Here you are. I want you write ‘I must not tell lies,’</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>How many times?</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Umbridge</b>: "<i>Oh, as long as it takes for the message to sink in</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Dolores Umbridge making Harry use the Blood Quill<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Umbridge_slap.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140912013700" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="130" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Umbridge slap.gif" data-image-key="Umbridge_slap.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Umbridge_slap.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140912013700" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Umbridge_slap.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140912013700" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Umbridge_slap.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140912013700" decoding="async" width="245" height="130" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Umbridge slap.gif" data-image-key="Umbridge_slap.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b4/Umbridge_slap.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140912013700" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Umbridge_slap.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Umbridge slaps Harry in a fit of anger</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>She showed a particular hatred for Harry Potter, as she had no qualms about violently punishing Harry during detentions (though it is possible Fudge told her to be harsh on him). During her year as a professor at Hogwarts, she acted as a disciplinarian, insisting the students to greet her loudly and clearly in a monotonous style at the beginning of every class, and answer her questions in the same manner.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite (or perhaps because of) her feigned politeness, the other teachers found her infuriating. Umbridge became more openly authoritative and cruel as she gained influence over the school, especially during her time as the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_High_Inquisitor" title="Hogwarts High Inquisitor">High Inquisitor</a>, as seen when she interrupted teachers with her leading questions, passive-aggressive comments, and disruptive note taking. She was especially insulting to Hagrid, whom she knew to be a "half-breed," and was blatantly condescending and rude to him during her inspection of his class. She interrupted Dumbledore during his speech at the <a href="/wiki/Start-of-Term_Feast" title="Start-of-Term Feast">Start-of-Term Feast</a>, and delivered a very dull speech while being ignorant of the students' restlessness, to the point that Harry angrily speculated that she would have continued with it even if a full-scale riot broke out under her nose.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Oh no, no, no. This is your punishment for spreading evil, nasty, attention seeking stories, Mr Potter, and punishments certainly cannot be adjusted to suit the guilty one’s convenience. No, you will come here at five o’clock tomorrow, and the next day, and on Friday too, and you will do your detentions as planned. I think it rather a good thing that you are missing something you really want to do. It ought to reinforce the lesson I am trying to teach you.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Umbridge justifying her cruel punishment on Harry Potter<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a9/Blood_quill.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140912015019" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="125" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Blood quill.gif" data-image-key="Blood_quill.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a9/Blood_quill.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140912015019" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a9/Blood_quill.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140912015019" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a9/Blood_quill.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140912015019" decoding="async" width="245" height="125" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Blood quill.gif" data-image-key="Blood_quill.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a9/Blood_quill.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140912015019" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Blood_quill.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry's hand due to Umbridge's punishments with the <a href="/wiki/Black_Quill" title="Black Quill">Black Quill</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>There were several signs indicating that Umbridge was impatient and had a short temper. However, she rarely expressed the extent of her anger openly, casually enforcing decrees written and signed by Fudge and handing out torturous punishments with a smile (most notably, forcing Harry to carve "I must not tell lies" into the back of his hand with a Black Quill) rather than openly taking out her hatred of children on the school as a whole. However, Umbridge's anger occasionally reached the surface when she did not feel things were as they should be, such as when Fred and George Weasley began a rebellion against her during her time as Headmistress, she had very little patience for the twins' antics. When <a href="/wiki/Marietta_Edgecombe" title="Marietta Edgecombe">Marietta Edgecombe</a>'s memories were secretly modified by <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Shacklebolt" title="Kingsley Shacklebolt">Kingsley Shacklebolt</a> and she did not tell the truth about <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>, Umbridge physically shook Marietta very hard, and only stopped when <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a> pointed his wand at her. She also had a tantrum when the gargoyle of the <a href="/wiki/Headmaster%27s_office" class="mw-redirect" title="Headmaster&#39;s office">Headmaster's office</a> refused to let her in when she became Headmistress, and an outburst against "half-breeds" led her to be carried away by centaurs in the Forbidden Forest.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)">"<i>You know... I really </i>hate<i> children.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Umbridge showing her true opinion of children<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Umbridge often made hypocritical statements, claiming during the Start-of-Term Feast that she assured the students that they would all be very good friends, she admitted later that she actually hated children, showing she had sacrificed a lot to do Fudge's bidding. Despite claiming to be a "tolerant woman", she frequently attempted to silence those with whom she disagreed. Her hatred of both "half-breeds" and "<a href="/wiki/Mudblood" title="Mudblood">Mudbloods</a>" demonstrated her intolerance, while her constantly shifting attachment to the currently most powerful showed her opportunism. Despite her incessant claims that telling lies was wrong, she was perfectly willing to lie herself, evidently without shame for it.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Her style of teaching students was also simply having them read from the textbook, while avoiding any practical lessons and answering students' questions, though she was simply following Fudge's orders on how to change Hogwarts. Indeed, Umbridge enforced his belief that theories were enough for students to get by exams and mastering self-defence, which in many situations proved both of them wrong, though she refused to acknowledge that fact. It is unclear if she ever agreed with it or if she merely had to keep her mouth shut as her opinions were of little consequence compared to the Minister of Magic.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite her wickedness and pure-blood supremacy attitude, Umbridge was repeatedly stated to be no Death Eater, as she never showed support for them until they took over the Ministry in 1997. She was fearful in response to the <a href="/wiki/Azkaban_escapes" title="Azkaban escapes">Azkaban breakout</a> in 1996 and was determined to capture <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> who was, at the time, believed to be a <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a>. Despite this, she was not above allying with them if it suited her interests. Once they took over she allied with them due to sharing many beliefs with them, as well as being given further power within the Ministry. It's also likely that she allied with them out of fear of being targeted as a high ranking Ministry official. Her support towards them only went so far however as she did not assist <a href="/wiki/Corban_Yaxley" title="Corban Yaxley">Yaxley</a> in pursuing Harry Potter and his friends when they infiltrated the Ministry, nor was she seen fighting in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>.
</p><p>Umbridge also understood the importance of <a href="/wiki/Argus_Filch" title="Argus Filch">Argus Filch</a>'s knowledge of the school's geography, and made efforts to befriend him in order to advantage herself, despite his status as a Squib, which many would consider a sign of a second-class citizen in the wizard community. However, she was not above blaming him for her own faults, to the point of irrationality, such as when she <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">stunned</a> one of the <a href="/wiki/Weasleys%27_Wildfire_Whiz-bangs" title="Weasleys&#39; Wildfire Whiz-bangs">Weasleys' Wildfire Whiz-bangs</a> causing it to explode, she called him out not to stun them despite his genetic inability to do so in the first place.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Umbridge also had an unhealthy habit of drinking a small cup of tea with three spoonfuls of <a href="/wiki/Sugar" title="Sugar">sugar</a>, which could have contributed to her gaining weight, and thus in all likelihood she had possessed the habit for a long time.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fd/Umbridge-2-.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160721184141" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Umbridge-2-.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge-2-.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fd/Umbridge-2-.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160721184141" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fd/Umbridge-2-.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160721184141" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fd/Umbridge-2-.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160721184141" decoding="async" width="250" height="141" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Umbridge-2-.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge-2-.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fd/Umbridge-2-.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160721184141" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Umbridge-2-.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">It is unclear if the Locket controlled her completely or partially, as Umbridge took to happily tormenting Muggle-borns under its influence</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The time Umbridge spent wearing Voldemort's locket exacerbated her worse qualities, to the extent that she was known to spout very uncharitable views on the non-magical community when intoxicated, to the point that even fellow pro-pure-blood coworkers were shocked by her. However, as it is never made clear how much influence the locket had on her mind, it may not be fair to judge her entirely for her actions with it on. For instance, her dislike of Muggle-borns increased into base cruelty, tormenting them with sham trials and sadistically sending them off to Azkaban. Her lack of control over her own mind is evidenced by the fact that she had no idea what she was wearing and so falsely claimed it was a family heirloom and proof of her relation to the <a href="/wiki/Selwyn_family" title="Selwyn family">Selwyn family</a>. She did not assist <a href="/wiki/Corban_Yaxley" title="Corban Yaxley">Yaxley</a> in chasing the trio when they infiltrated the Ministry. She also mounted plaques on her office doors to display her political titles.<sup id="cite_ref-DH13_5-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH13-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Magical_abilities_and_skills">Magical abilities and skills</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=18" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Magical abilities and skills">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Magical abilities and skills"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>The Cruciatus Curse might loosen your tongue.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Dolores threatening <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> with dark magic<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 122px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/ba/Umbridge_cat_Patronus.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20131229055316" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="120" height="258" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Umbridge cat Patronus.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge_cat_Patronus.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/ba/Umbridge_cat_Patronus.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/120?cb=20131229055316" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/ba/Umbridge_cat_Patronus.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20131229055316" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/ba/Umbridge_cat_Patronus.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/120?cb=20131229055316" decoding="async" width="120" height="258" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Umbridge cat Patronus.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge_cat_Patronus.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/ba/Umbridge_cat_Patronus.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/120?cb=20131229055316" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Umbridge_cat_Patronus.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Umbridge's <a href="/wiki/Persian_cat" title="Persian cat">Persian cat</a> <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Despite her high ranking position in the Ministry, at first glance Umbridge did not appear to be a particularly powerful witch. She had no knowledge of the brewing process for <a href="/wiki/Veritaserum" title="Veritaserum">Veritaserum</a> and because she needed it (and unwisely squandered a bottle full on one interrogation although she had been told that it was not necessary), it is unlikely that she was a <a href="/wiki/Legilimency" title="Legilimency">Legilimens</a>. She also could not eliminate the <a href="/wiki/Weasleys%27_Wildfire_Whiz-bangs" title="Weasleys&#39; Wildfire Whiz-bangs">Weasleys' Wildfire Whiz-bangs</a> and their <a href="/wiki/Portable_Swamp" title="Portable Swamp">Portable Swamp</a>, feats that other professors easily did (which they refused to at first, just to give Umbridge trouble). She was also unable to remove <a href="/wiki/Marietta_Edgecombe" title="Marietta Edgecombe">Marietta Edgecombe</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army_parchment_jinx" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army parchment jinx">"SNEAK" pimple formation</a>, implying that she may not have been very skilled with <a href="/wiki/Counter-jinx" title="Counter-jinx">counter-jinxes</a> (although it is possible that no counter-jinx existed for Hermione's spell).<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Her real <a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">magical</a> power and knowledge were mainly focused in offensive and defensive magic, particularly of a darker variety. 
</p>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Charm" title="Charm">Charms</a></b>:  Umbridge was shown to be proficient with charm-work. She could cast charms such as the <a href="/wiki/Blackboard_Writing_Spell" title="Blackboard Writing Spell">Blackboard Writing Spell</a>, <a href="/wiki/Parchment-sealing_spell" title="Parchment-sealing spell">Parchment-sealing spell</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fire-Making_Spell" title="Fire-Making Spell">Fire-Making Spell</a>, <a href="/wiki/Shield_Charm" title="Shield Charm">Shield Charm</a> and <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">Stunning Spell</a> successfully and effortlessly.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-OOTPF_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTPF-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> She also used a <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge%27s_neatness_charm" title="Dolores Umbridge&#39;s neatness charm">charm</a> to neaten the uniforms of Hogwarts students, much to their irritation.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTPF_14-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTPF-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> She could perform the highly advanced <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus Charm</a> even under the influence of Dark Magic; in fact, due to her malice and the <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Locket" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Locket">locket</a> <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a> being compatible with one other, her Patronus was strengthened by <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort's</a> fragmented <a href="/wiki/Soul" title="Soul">soul</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-online_bloomsbury_chat_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-online_bloomsbury_chat-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> It took the form of a <a href="/wiki/Persian_cat" title="Persian cat">Persian cat</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH13_5-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH13-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a></b>: Umbridge was sure of her ability to cast the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a>, which would require the desire to inflict harm on the victim, her sadism being a perfect prerequisite.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> She invented the <a href="/wiki/Black_Quill" title="Black Quill">Black Quill</a> sometime before <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-pottermoreprofile_1-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermoreprofile-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> a dark magical torture device that cut the words written with it into the writer's hand, which she utilised heavily for punishing dissident students while she was working at Hogwarts,<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> showing she was skilled with handling dark artefacts. The fact that she was able to craft such a malicious object capable of inflicting much plain and displeasure upon its victims implies she had a great amount of talent in dark magic, as it was even capable of leaving physical scars. Furthermore, she had considerable skill with handling and commanding <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a>, known dark <a href="/wiki/Creature" title="Creature">creatures</a>. She successfully ordered several Dementors <a href="/wiki/Attack_in_Little_Whinging" title="Attack in Little Whinging">to attack and attempt to murder Harry Potter and Dudley Dursley</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 233px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/05/Incarcerous.gif/revision/latest?cb=20160822065707" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="231" height="130" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Incarcerous.gif" data-image-key="Incarcerous.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/05/Incarcerous.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/231?cb=20160822065707" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/05/Incarcerous.gif/revision/latest?cb=20160822065707" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/05/Incarcerous.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/231?cb=20160822065707" decoding="async" width="231" height="130" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Incarcerous.gif" data-image-key="Incarcerous.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/05/Incarcerous.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/231?cb=20160822065707" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Incarcerous.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Umbridge conjuring ropes, an advanced form of transfiguration</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">Transfiguration</a></b>:  She was able to effectively <a href="/wiki/Conjuration" title="Conjuration">conjure</a> ropes at a moment's notice with the <a href="/wiki/Incarcerous_Spell" title="Incarcerous Spell">Incarcerous Spell</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> which is an advanced form of Transfiguration, as <a href="/wiki/Conjuration" title="Conjuration">conjuration</a> can only be performed by those who are proficient in this highly difficult branch of <a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">magic</a>. Umbridge was also capable of conjuring glasses and cups of various drinks, which she offered to Harry Potter at one time in her office.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Nonverbal_spell" title="Nonverbal spell">Nonverbal magic</a></b>: She could <a href="/wiki/Blackboard_Writing_Spell" title="Blackboard Writing Spell">write on a blackboard</a>, turn out books and <a href="/wiki/Fire-Making_Spell" title="Fire-Making Spell">burn</a> a paper, all by just raising or pointing her wand. She also offered Harry Potter drinks with Veritaserum in it by just flicking her wand and was capable of casting a non-verbal <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">Stunning Spell</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> She was also capable of casting a non-verbal <a href="/wiki/Revulsion_Jinx" title="Revulsion Jinx">Revulsion Jinx</a>, which she used to often harass students during her time at Hogwarts.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTPF_14-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTPF-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Duelling" title="Duelling">Duelling</a></b>: Although her skills as a duellist is unknown, she showed no fear in attempting to subdue <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> albeit with <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a>, <a href="/wiki/John_Dawlish" title="John Dawlish">John Dawlish</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Shacklebolt" title="Kingsley Shacklebolt">Kingsley Shacklebolt</a> (the latter two being <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Aurors</a>) backing her up, suggesting that she may have had some skill in this field. However, as was easily predictable from the beginning, Dumbledore effortlessly defeated her and all of her ministry compatriots with a single spell far faster before they could even draw their wands against Dumbledore.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Possessions">Possessions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=19" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Possessions">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Possessions"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 202px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d8/Baguette_d%27Ombrage.png/revision/latest?cb=20150317162259" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="200" height="74" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Baguette d&#39;Ombrage.png" data-image-key="Baguette_d&#39;Ombrage.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d8/Baguette_d%27Ombrage.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20150317162259" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d8/Baguette_d%27Ombrage.png/revision/latest?cb=20150317162259" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d8/Baguette_d%27Ombrage.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20150317162259" decoding="async" width="200" height="74" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Baguette d&#39;Ombrage.png" data-image-key="Baguette_d&#39;Ombrage.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d8/Baguette_d%27Ombrage.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20150317162259" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Baguette_d%27Ombrage.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dolores Umbridge's wand</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d3/Dolores_Umbridge%27s_Enchanted_Quill_concept_art.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180708164857" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="290" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dolores Umbridge&#39;s Enchanted Quill concept art.jpg" data-image-key="Dolores_Umbridge&#39;s_Enchanted_Quill_concept_art.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d3/Dolores_Umbridge%27s_Enchanted_Quill_concept_art.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180708164857" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d3/Dolores_Umbridge%27s_Enchanted_Quill_concept_art.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180708164857" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d3/Dolores_Umbridge%27s_Enchanted_Quill_concept_art.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180708164857" decoding="async" width="180" height="290" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dolores Umbridge&#39;s Enchanted Quill concept art.jpg" data-image-key="Dolores_Umbridge&#39;s_Enchanted_Quill_concept_art.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d3/Dolores_Umbridge%27s_Enchanted_Quill_concept_art.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180708164857" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dolores_Umbridge%27s_Enchanted_Quill_concept_art.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Her Black Quill</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge%27s_wand" title="Dolores Umbridge&#39;s wand">Wand</a></b>: Umbridge owned a wand made of <a href="/wiki/Birch" title="Birch">birch</a> and <a href="/wiki/Dragon_heartstring" title="Dragon heartstring">dragon heartstring</a>. It is noted for being unusually short in length, only eight inches. It was snapped in half when a <a href="/wiki/Centaur" title="Centaur">Centaur</a> stomped on it in the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> She got a replacement, as she was able to cast a Patronus Charm more than one year later, but this wand was confiscated when she was arrested.<sup id="cite_ref-DH13_5-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH13-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Garrick_Ollivander" title="Garrick Ollivander">Garrick Ollivander</a> also noted that wands unusually short in length are often destined for those that have something lacking in character.<sup id="cite_ref-wandlength_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-wandlength-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Frolicsome_Feline_plates" title="Frolicsome Feline plates">Frolicsome Feline plates</a></b>: Dolores owned many ornamental kitten plates which she hung all along the walls of her <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts_Professor%27s_office" class="mw-redirect" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts Professor&#39;s office">office</a> at Hogwarts School, as well as her <a href="/wiki/Senior_Undersecretary_to_the_Minister_for_Magic%27s_office" title="Senior Undersecretary to the Minister for Magic&#39;s office">office</a> at the Ministry.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-DH13_5-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH13-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Black_Quill" title="Black Quill">Black Quill</a></b>: Umbridge owned at least one Blood Quill which she used as a method of punishment. She had students who displeased her write lines using a <a href="/wiki/Blood" title="Blood">blood</a> quill, which Minerva McGonagall considered a "medieval method" of punishment.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> This quill was her <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">dark</a> own invention.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermoreprofile_1-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermoreprofile-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Locket" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Locket">Salazar Slytherin's Locket</a></b>: Umbridge accepted the locket from <a href="/wiki/Mundungus_Fletcher" title="Mundungus Fletcher">Mundungus Fletcher</a> as a bribe, but did not know that it was one of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>, nor that it was once <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin" title="Salazar Slytherin">Salazar Slytherin</a>'s heirloom. She instead used the ornate "S" to falsely claim that it was an heirloom of the <a href="/wiki/Selwyn_family" title="Selwyn family">Selwyn family</a>, to bolster her pure-blood credentials. It was taken by <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and <a href="/wiki/Doubling_Charm" title="Doubling Charm">replaced with a fake</a> by <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH13_5-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH13-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> The locket's evil was what increased her magical strength to the point of being able to produce a Patronus, because she was already evil.<sup id="cite_ref-online_bloomsbury_chat_21-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-online_bloomsbury_chat-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=20" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Relationships">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Relationships"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Family">Family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=21" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Family">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Family"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Dolores was born a half-blood to wizard <a href="/wiki/Orford_Umbridge" title="Orford Umbridge">Orford Umbridge</a> and muggle <a href="/wiki/Ellen_Cracknell" title="Ellen Cracknell">Ellen Cracknell</a>, and has a <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge%27s_brother" title="Dolores Umbridge&#39;s brother">younger brother</a>, who is a <a href="/wiki/Squib" title="Squib">squib</a>.
</p><p>Under the influence of her father, Dolores blamed her mother for being the cause to her brother being born without magical powers, as well as looking down on said brother. Coupled with Ellen's flightiness and untidiness, Dolores came to hate both her mother and brother. She considered them to be inferior and upon reaching 15 years old, she and her father remained in the wizarding world, while Ellen took her son and returned to the Muggle world, never seeing each other again.
</p><p>Although her father was the source of influence on her prejudiced views on blood purity, Dolores found him rather irksome for his unambitious nature as a janitorial worker at the bottom of the social ladder. While climbing the ranks in the Ministry herself, Dolores found her father to be a source of embarrassment, and pressured him into an early retirement, disappearing from public sight in exchange for the promise of a small monthly allowance. With her father silently removed from public, Dolores managed to give herself a better public image.
