Whenever her colleagues (mostly the ones who disliked her) asked if she was related to the Umbridge who used to mop floors, she would use her sweetest smile (which indicates her suppressed rage) to deny all connections, and falsely claimed that her deceased father was an esteemed member of the Wizengamot. Nasty things tended to happen to people who asked about Orford, or anything else Dolores did not want to talk about, so people who wished to be on her good side would pretend to believe her false heritage. Once Dolores was arrested and sentenced to Azkaban, Orford lost his pittance that his daughter gave him.
</p><p>Ambitious and prejudiced, Dolores was utterly disgusted with all three of her family members, having no love for any of them, dismissing them and severing all ties with them due to their low birth and/or poor social statuses, and never again speaking about any of them. She then lied to others being a pure-blood, seeing herself as such, and even falsely connecting herself to the prestigious <a href="/wiki/Selwyn_family" title="Selwyn family">Selwyn family</a>, to bolster her pure-blood credentials and cover her shameful heritage.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Harry_Potter">Harry Potter</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=22" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Harry Potter">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Harry Potter"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>The Cruciatus Curse ought to loosen your tongue. What Cornelius doesn’t know won’t hurt him. He never knew I ordered dementors after Potter last summer, but he was delighted to be given the chance to expel him, all the same. . . .</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Umbridge explaining her hatred of and willingness to torture Harry Potter<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9a/OOTP_promo_front_Harry_cropped.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190106225911" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="251" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="OOTP promo front Harry cropped.jpg" data-image-key="OOTP_promo_front_Harry_cropped.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9a/OOTP_promo_front_Harry_cropped.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190106225911" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9a/OOTP_promo_front_Harry_cropped.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190106225911" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9a/OOTP_promo_front_Harry_cropped.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190106225911" decoding="async" width="180" height="251" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="OOTP promo front Harry cropped.jpg" data-image-key="OOTP_promo_front_Harry_cropped.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9a/OOTP_promo_front_Harry_cropped.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190106225911" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:OOTP_promo_front_Harry_cropped.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, her enemy and former student</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Dolores Umbridge did everything in her power to make Harry Potter's life as miserable as possible, and thus, the two of them had a mutual loathing for each other. In the summer of <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, Umbridge sent two <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a> after Harry and his cousin <a href="/wiki/Dudley_Dursley" title="Dudley Dursley">Dudley</a>. This was an attempt to silence him from contradicting the Ministry's official opinion that Voldemort had not returned. Umbridge was one of Harry's jurors when he was summoned to the Ministry for a trial of the underage magic he used to fend off the Dementors, and she wanted him to be convicted, but he was acquitted due to the efforts of <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> and <a href="/wiki/Arabella_Figg" title="Arabella Figg">Arabella Figg</a>.
</p><p>With Dolores Umbridge as his new <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> teacher, Harry found himself hating Umbridge the moment he set his eyes on her, from her fluffy pink cardigan to her high-pitched girlish voice, despite not having an actual reason at the time. He often was outspoken in class and suffered for his inability to control his temper; he served detention several times with her during that year in which he would be forced to write lines with his own blood using a <a href="/wiki/Black_Quill" title="Black Quill">Blood Quill</a>, which magically scarred Harry's hand. <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a> was highly critical of Umbridge's methods, and warned Harry not to cross her because he would get into big trouble at school, and, possibly, even with the Ministry. Before Umbridge, Harry thought there would never be a teacher he hated as much as <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, but found Umbridge to be a strong contender.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Harry felt a strong urge to swing around and seize her by the throat</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Harry Potter furious at Umbridge for calling <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a> a "great half-breed oaf"<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Using her newly acquired power under the Educational Decrees from the Ministry, she banned all extra-curricular activities and gatherings until they were approved by the High Inquisitor (herself); this meant that the House Quidditch teams were disbanded. Slytherin's team was immediately reinstated while Gryffindor was delayed from reforming for nearly a month after then-captain <a href="/wiki/Angelina_Johnson" title="Angelina Johnson">Angelina Johnson</a> put in the request. As well as making Harry use a quill that would slice open his hand and cause him to write in his own blood, she banned Harry, Fred, and George from playing <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> later in the year after they attacked <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> (though their bans were all lifted following Umbridge's eventual removal from Hogwarts) for his cruel insults.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/Detention_dolores.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150824223903" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="167" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Detention dolores.jpg" data-image-key="Detention_dolores.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/Detention_dolores.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150824223903" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/Detention_dolores.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150824223903" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/Detention_dolores.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150824223903" decoding="async" width="250" height="167" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Detention dolores.jpg" data-image-key="Detention_dolores.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c4/Detention_dolores.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150824223903" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Detention_dolores.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dolores forcing Harry to write lines with his own blood as ink during a detention</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Umbridge monitored all incoming and outgoing mail, and Harry's owl <a href="/wiki/Hedwig" title="Hedwig">Hedwig</a> was injured on Umbridge's orders. She made it difficult for Harry, Ron, and Hermione to visit Hagrid. When Rita Skeeter published an article in <i><a href="/wiki/The_Quibbler" title="The Quibbler">The Quibbler</a></i> about Harry's past experiences with Voldemort during the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a>, Dolores banned Harry from trips to Hogsmeade. Umbridge nearly used the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a> to get Harry to talk before Hermione intervened and, together with Harry, tricked Umbridge into going into the Forest to show her "Dumbledore's weapon". This resulted in Umbridge being carried off by the centaurs, whom she had attacked first, due to her hatred of half-breeds.
</p><p>After the Ministry had finally acknowledged Voldemort's return to power, Umbridge was removed from Hogwarts. However, Harry was furious to learn later that year that Umbridge was still working for the Ministry of Magic. The next year Lord Voldemort took over the Ministry. Umbridge showed her respect for Lord Voldemort and the Death Eaters by taking part in the hunt for Harry Potter. She branded Harry as "Undesirable No.1,"  and was given the job of Head of the <a href="/wiki/Muggle-Born_Registration_Commission" title="Muggle-Born Registration Commission">Muggle-Born Registration Commission</a>. This was a job that involved sadistically sentencing innocent Muggle-borns to Azkaban on the false charge of stealing magic. Harry learned that Umbridge had one of Voldemort's Horcruxes and <a href="/wiki/Mad_Eye_Moody%27s_magical_eye" class="mw-redirect" title="Mad Eye Moody&#39;s magical eye">Mad Eye Moody's magical eye</a> in her possession. During the <a href="/wiki/Infiltration_of_the_British_Ministry_of_Magic_(1997)" title="Infiltration of the British Ministry of Magic (1997)">Infiltration of the Ministry of Magic</a>, Harry saw Umbridge ruthlessly interrogating a poor Muggle-born. Enraged, Harry stunned Umbridge and retrieved the Horcrux. He also took the eye from her office and buried it.
</p><p>Given Harry's grudge against her, it is likely that he provided testimony against her during her trial before being given a life sentence in Azkaban. 
</p><p>In the Alternative Reality created by Harry's son, Albus, and his friend, Scorpius Malfoy, it was found that Umbridge seemed delighted in Harry's death in May 1998. The delight of it extended to the point where she wished that he did not rest in peace but in endless despair in the Voldemort controlled world.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Cornelius_Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=23" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Cornelius Fudge">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Cornelius Fudge"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>What Cornelius doesn't know won't hurt him.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Umbridge before she attempts to torture <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> with the illegal <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a>, showing her view of Fudge<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d9/Cornelius_Fudge_2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20131029103809" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="288" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Cornelius Fudge 2.jpg" data-image-key="Cornelius_Fudge_2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d9/Cornelius_Fudge_2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20131029103809" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d9/Cornelius_Fudge_2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20131029103809" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d9/Cornelius_Fudge_2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20131029103809" decoding="async" width="180" height="288" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Cornelius Fudge 2.jpg" data-image-key="Cornelius_Fudge_2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d9/Cornelius_Fudge_2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20131029103809" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Cornelius_Fudge_2.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Minister of Magic, <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a>, her superior</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Umbridge was Cornelius Fudge's right-hand woman, being his Senior-Undersecretary, and he trusted her greatly to place her into Hogwarts to control it. He granted her many powers through <a href="/wiki/Educational_Decree" title="Educational Decree">Educational Decrees</a>, and full-heartedly agreed with all of her comments and mockeries against Dumbledore and Harry.
</p><p>Fudge seemed to be unaware of Umbridge's dark and sadistic nature. In return, Umbridge was loyal to Fudge only because of the power he was offering her, and felt no true attachments to the misguided man. She was also willing to break the law behind the Minister's back to achieve results, such as summoning <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a> in an attempt to expel Harry, as well as attempting to use the illegal <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a> for interrogation, all the while stating that "<i>what Cornelius doesn't know won't hurt him.</i>" Umbridge was always an opportunist seeking for power and status, and when Cornelius was succumbing to paranoia in 1995, she took full advantage by stoking the Minister's vanity and fears, feigning sympathy for his anxiety in order to use him for promotions. When Fudge was dismissed, Umbridge stood beside the new Ministers instead, even when it became apparent that the new regime established in 1997 was morally corrupt (which actually fell in line with her true personality).
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ministry_of_Magic">Ministry of Magic</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=24" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Ministry of Magic">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Ministry of Magic"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>As the Senior Undersecretary of the Minister for Magic, Umbridge was incredibly supportive of the aims of her superiors, Ministers <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Fudge</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rufus_Scrimgeour" title="Rufus Scrimgeour">Scrimgeour</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Pius_Thicknesse" title="Pius Thicknesse">Thicknesse</a>. During their respective downfalls, however, Umbridge did not try to stand up for them, meaning that she only served them loyally for the power that she was offered, and felt no true attachments towards any of them. Some of her equals also respected her enough. In fact, <a href="/wiki/Percy_Weasley" title="Percy Weasley">Percy Weasley</a> sent a letter to his younger brother, stating that Umbridge was a "truly delightful woman", and that Ron should side with her instead of continuing to associate with Harry. However, others, like <a href="/wiki/Amelia_Bones" title="Amelia Bones">Amelia Bones</a> and <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Arthur Weasley</a>, didn't appear to like her. Furthermore, some lower-ranking employees tended to talk ill of her behind her back, as seen when she was the <a href="/wiki/Head_of_the_Muggle-Born_Registration_Commission" title="Head of the Muggle-Born Registration Commission">Head of the Muggle-Born Registration Commission</a>, when some pamphlet makers complained about her usage of Alastor Moody's magical eye to monitor them. She mainly keeps up the facade of a respectable official amongst most of her equals and superiors, but has no trouble tyrannising her subordinates.
</p><p>During her earlier years, she attempted to charm her superiors for a marriage, in order to raise her status and power, but, while they valued her hard work and ambitions, they knew her enough that they found her very difficult to like and refused to have any affectionate relationship with her. Some of her coworkers who dislike her tend to ask her if she is related to <a href="/wiki/Orford_Umbridge" title="Orford Umbridge">the Umbridge</a> who used to mop floors at the Ministry, which she took offensively before denying it, and caused some nasty events to happen to such people, thus leading to those who wished to remain on her good side to believe her invented ancestry. After the Ministry was reformed under <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Shacklebolt" title="Kingsley Shacklebolt">Kingsley Shacklebolt</a>'s guidance, Umbridge was arrested, tried and imprisoned for her crimes against Muggle-borns, as not all the Muggle-borns she sent to Azkaban survived their imprisonment during the Second Wizarding War.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Minerva_McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=25" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Minerva McGonagall">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Minerva McGonagall"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Minerva McGonagall</b>: "<i>He has achieved high marks in all of his Defence against the Dark Arts tests —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Umbridge</b>: "<i>I'm terribly sorry to have to contradict you, Minerva, but as you will see from my note, Harry has been achieving very poor results in his classes with me —</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Minerva McGonagall</b>: "<i>I should have made my meaning plainer... He has achieved high marks in all Defence Against the Dark Arts tests set by a </i>competent<i> teacher.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; McGonagall arguing with Umbridge in regards to Harry Potter<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150810172040" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="255" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Mcgonagall.jpg" data-image-key="Mcgonagall.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150810172040" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150810172040" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150810172040" decoding="async" width="180" height="255" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Mcgonagall.jpg" data-image-key="Mcgonagall.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Mcgonagall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150810172040" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Mcgonagall.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>, her enemy</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Minerva McGonagall disliked Dolores Umbridge from the beginning, and their relationship only worsened over time. When the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> teacher began to invade Hogwarts with her <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_High_Inquisitor" title="Hogwarts High Inquisitor">Hogwarts High Inquisitor</a> position, she did everything she could in her power to circumvent Umbridge's authority without risking the loss of her job. During Umbridge's inspections of McGonagall's class, Minerva tried for the most part to ignore Dolores. This was difficult, due to Umbridge's constant interruptions of McGonagall using her signature soft, girlish cough of "<i>Hem hem</i>". When forced to acknowledge Umbridge's presence, McGonagall treated her with a cold and harsh demeanour, much to the pleasure of many students.
</p><p>Although Dolores had the authority to put Minerva on probation or even sack her, Minerva was not afraid to show her disgust and hatred of Dolores to her face. Despite this, she understood that Umbridge had a lot of power and that she was reporting directly to <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a>, and so Minerva once warned <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> to tread carefully around Umbridge. Even so, she vehemently vouched for Harry during their <a href="/wiki/Careers_Advice" title="Careers Advice">Career Advice</a> session, claiming that she would coach him nightly if she had to in order to realise his dream of becoming an <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a>, after Umbridge's furiously protested that Harry would never become one; during this session, Minerva indirectly claimed Dolores' evaluation as incompetent and would not be taken into consideration. After Umbridge fired <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Sybill Trelawney</a> from her post as <a href="/wiki/Divination" title="Divination">Divination</a> teacher, Minerva even put aside her mild dislike of Sybill to focus even more on her hatred of Dolores.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c1/Mcgonagalleumbridge.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160721195022" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="166" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Mcgonagalleumbridge.jpg" data-image-key="Mcgonagalleumbridge.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c1/Mcgonagalleumbridge.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160721195022" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c1/Mcgonagalleumbridge.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160721195022" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c1/Mcgonagalleumbridge.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160721195022" decoding="async" width="250" height="166" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Mcgonagalleumbridge.jpg" data-image-key="Mcgonagalleumbridge.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c1/Mcgonagalleumbridge.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160721195022" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Mcgonagalleumbridge.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dolores and Minerva tensely stand next to each other</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Even when Dolores took over Hogwarts, replacing <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> as head of the school, Minerva continued to help undermine Umbridge's reign, preferring to watch her struggle with the chaos that was being caused by the students and Peeves (sometimes she even helped with it). When Minerva attempted to prevent the attack on Hagrid, Umbridge and her cohorts shot her down with four simultaneous Stunners, severely injuring her, requiring her to be sent to <a href="/wiki/St_Mungo%27s_Hospital_for_Magical_Maladies_and_Injuries" title="St Mungo&#39;s Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries">St Mungo's Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries</a> Dolores was pleased at this, as it meant she had full control of Hogwarts. After Minerva's return to Hogwarts, Minerva did nothing to curb the students' enthusiasm when <a href="/wiki/Peeves" title="Peeves">Peeves</a> chased Dolores from Hogwarts, only lamenting that she could not run after Umbridge herself (because the poltergeist had taken her walking stick to hit Dolores with as he followed her from the school).
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Fred_and_George_Weasley">Fred and George Weasley</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=26" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Fred and George Weasley">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Fred and George Weasley"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Fred Weasley</b>: "<i>We won't be seeing you!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>George Weasley</b>: "<i>Yeah, don't bother to keep in touch.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Fred Weasley</b>: "<i>If anybody fancies buying a Portable Swamp, as demonstrated upstairs, come to number ninety-three Diagon Alley — <a href="/wiki/Weasley%27s_Wizard_Wheezes" class="mw-redirect" title="Weasley&#39;s Wizard Wheezes">Weasley's Wizard Wheezes</a>. Our new premises!</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>George Weasley</b>: "<i>Special discounts to Hogwarts students who swear they're going to use our products to get rid of this old bat!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Fred and George depart Hogwarts giving their last sentiments to Umbridge<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d4/Fred%26George.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080904172253" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="134" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Fred&amp;George.jpg" data-image-key="Fred&amp;George.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d4/Fred%26George.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20080904172253" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d4/Fred%26George.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080904172253" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d4/Fred%26George.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20080904172253" decoding="async" width="180" height="134" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Fred&amp;George.jpg" data-image-key="Fred&amp;George.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d4/Fred%26George.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20080904172253" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Fred%26George.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Fred and George Weasley, her former students whom she particularly despised</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Fred and George Weasley hated Umbridge, who was appointed by the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> as the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> professor in 1995. Umbridge was a sadistic woman who enjoyed punishing and torturing students. Almost every resident of Hogwarts at the time hated Umbridge, but she particularly hated <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, Fred and George. When George and Harry attacked <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> after a Gryffindor — Slytherin <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> match, Umbridge kicked them off the team, along with Fred.
</p><p>Fred and George were the only ones who opposed Umbridge. They developed special fireworks and set them off within the castle after Umbridge was appointed Head of Hogwarts. The fireworks took fantastical forms, such as a monstrous light dragon and Catherine wheels. They also created a <a href="/wiki/Portable_Swamp" title="Portable Swamp">Portable Swamp</a>, which was commended by Charms Professor <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Filius Flitwick</a> as a bit of "<i>really good magic</i>," in order to anger Umbridge just before leaving Hogwarts. When she attempted to punish them, Fred and George insulted her in front of the whole school and then fled with their broomsticks, much to her absolute fury, as she ordered her <a href="/wiki/Inquisitorial_Squad" title="Inquisitorial Squad">Inquisitorial Squad</a> to apprehend the two, which failed. In response, the twins "strongly suggested" that Peeves "<i>give her hell from us</i>" before flying out of the castle grounds, a departure that would become somewhat of a legend at the school.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Inquisitorial_Squad">Inquisitorial Squad</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=27" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Inquisitorial Squad">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Inquisitorial Squad"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/10/InquisitorialSquadDiscovery.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180627014358" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="InquisitorialSquadDiscovery.jpg" data-image-key="InquisitorialSquadDiscovery.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/10/InquisitorialSquadDiscovery.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180627014358" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/10/InquisitorialSquadDiscovery.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180627014358" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/10/InquisitorialSquadDiscovery.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180627014358" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="InquisitorialSquadDiscovery.jpg" data-image-key="InquisitorialSquadDiscovery.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/10/InquisitorialSquadDiscovery.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180627014358" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:InquisitorialSquadDiscovery.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Umbridge with the Inquisitorial Squad</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Some of the Slytherin students as well as the caretaker, <a href="/wiki/Argus_Filch" title="Argus Filch">Argus Filch</a>, happily supported Umbridge during her reign as the High Inquisitor and later Headmistress of Hogwarts; relating her cruelty and sadism with their own ambitions. In fact, Filch claimed that Umbridge was the best thing to happen to Hogwarts, falling for her ploy to gain his trust by rewarding him with, for example, permission to use torture as a form of punishment.
</p><p>However, Umbridge was fully aware that she could rely only on herself in the more crucial situations, evidenced in her reaction to <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>'s greedy facial expression upon hearing of Dumbledore's fabled "secret weapon" from an apparently distraught <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>. Umbridge, believing Hermione's bluff, then took it upon herself to discover this weapon first-hand rather than send one of her Slytherin cronies to do it for her. Other members of the <a href="/wiki/Inquisitorial_Squad" title="Inquisitorial Squad">Inquisitorial Squad</a> were <a href="/wiki/Pansy_Parkinson" title="Pansy Parkinson">Pansy Parkinson</a>, <a href="/wiki/Millicent_Bulstrode" title="Millicent Bulstrode">Millicent Bulstrode</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vincent_Crabbe" title="Vincent Crabbe">Vincent Crabbe</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gregory_Goyle" title="Gregory Goyle">Gregory Goyle</a>, <a href="/wiki/Graham_Montague" title="Graham Montague">Graham Montague</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Cassius_Warrington" title="Cassius Warrington">C. Warrington</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Severus_Snape">Severus Snape</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=28" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Severus Snape">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Severus Snape"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Umbridge</b>: "<i>Now . . . how long have you been teaching at Hogwarts?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Snape</b>: "<i>Fourteen years</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Umbridge</b>: "<i>You applied first for the Defence Against the Dark Arts post, I believe?</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Snape</b>: "<i>Yes</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Umbridge</b>: "<i>But you were unsuccessful?</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Snape</b>: "<i>Obviously</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Umbridge patronising Snape during her class inspections<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081103135333" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="254" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Severus Snape Profile.jpg" data-image-key="Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20081103135333" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081103135333" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20081103135333" decoding="async" width="180" height="254" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Severus Snape Profile.jpg" data-image-key="Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20081103135333" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, who disliked Umbridge immensely</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The only Slytherin who did not support Dolores Umbridge during her tenure at Hogwarts was the <a href="/wiki/Head_of_Slytherin_House" title="Head of Slytherin House">Head of Slytherin House</a> himself, Severus Snape. Like Harry, Snape hated Umbridge from the moment he set eyes on her for taking the post of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> teacher. Like his colleagues, he did as little to help her as possible due to seeing her as the spoiled child she was. Because of this, Snape was the only one who could ignore Umbridge's insults and endure her tantrums. He was, however, not above subtle taunting as shown when he merely raised an eyebrow after she told him he was on probation or when he pointed out the foolishness in her use of the entire bottle of <a href="/wiki/Veritaserum" title="Veritaserum">Veritaserum</a> (which was fake) he gave her when she only needed three drops.
</p><p>Umbridge in turn seemed to enjoy bullying Snape over the fact that Dumbledore always refused him the Defence Against the Dark Arts position, which Snape found to be infuriating, and barely hid his rage. She was also annoyed with his lack of support for her and accused him of being "deliberately unhelpful". In general Umbridge seemed to expect more support from Snape, due to <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a> speaking highly of him to her.
</p><p>In an <a href="/wiki/Alternate_reality" title="Alternate reality">alternate reality</a> in which Voldemort won the war and Umbridge became the official Headmistress of Hogwarts, she kept Snape as a teacher of the school. Umbridge claimed that she knew of Snape's true allegiance to the Order of the Phoenix for years, but did not act on it at the time; it was only when Severus assisted <a href="/wiki/Scorpius_Malfoy" title="Scorpius Malfoy">Scorpius Malfoy</a> in defying Voldemort did Umbridge expressed her regret of not dealing with Snape before. In short, it seems Umbridge kept Snape around for his teaching capabilities while disregarding his loyalty as something that could not bring harm to the new regime until he made an open move. Snape, in turn, had no qualms in blasting Umbridge back when she confronted them.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Horace_Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=29" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Horace Slughorn">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Horace Slughorn"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Another Slytherin who never liked Umbridge was her Head of House Horace Slughorn; he did not nominate her to be <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">Prefect</a> nor <a href="/wiki/Head_Boy_or_Girl" title="Head Boy or Girl">Head Girl</a>. He did not hesitate to express how he always considered her an "idiotic woman" and admitted that he never liked her in front of Harry, especially after hearing she foolishly called a <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest_Centaur_colony" title="Forbidden Forest Centaur colony">herd</a> of <a href="/wiki/Centaur" title="Centaur">centaur</a> "filthy <a href="/wiki/Half-breed" title="Half-breed">half-breeds</a>". Harry, sharing this contemptuous dislike for Umbridge, chuckled at Horace's comment.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_Hogwarts_residents_and_teachers">Other Hogwarts residents and teachers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=30" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Other Hogwarts residents and teachers">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Other Hogwarts residents and teachers"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Sybill Trelawney</b>: "<i>No! NO! This cannot be happening... It cannot... I refuse to accept it!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Umbridge</b>: "<i>You didn't realise this was coming? Incapable though you are of predicting even tomorrow's weather, you must surely have realised that your pitiful performance during my inspections, and lack of any improvement, would make it inevitable you would be sacked?</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Dolores Umbrige, soundly callously amused, insulting Trelawney while she sacks her<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7a/Umbridge_sacks_Trelawney_1996.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150816123805" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Umbridge sacks Trelawney 1996.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge_sacks_Trelawney_1996.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7a/Umbridge_sacks_Trelawney_1996.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150816123805" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7a/Umbridge_sacks_Trelawney_1996.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150816123805" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7a/Umbridge_sacks_Trelawney_1996.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150816123805" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Umbridge sacks Trelawney 1996.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge_sacks_Trelawney_1996.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7a/Umbridge_sacks_Trelawney_1996.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150816123805" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Umbridge_sacks_Trelawney_1996.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Umbridge sacking <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Professor Trelawney</a> and attempting to send her away from <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Castle" title="Hogwarts Castle">Hogwarts Castle</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During her time as a student, Umbridge never truly enjoyed her time at Hogwarts, and being denied any position of power (i.e. Prefect, Head Girl) made her resent the establishment. Upon being installed by Fudge as a teacher, Umbridge saw it as a golden opportunity to get revenge against the school that did not (as she saw it) give her her due respect.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermoreprofile_1-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermoreprofile-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>While at Hogwarts as a staff member, Dolores Umbridge was, overall, a highly unpleasant person to be around. As such, she was highly unpopular to most students and teachers in <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> school. In fact, she was despised or feared by many of the other residents of the grounds, such as the Ghosts, Paintings, House Elves, and the Forbidden Forest Centaurs. She would constantly interrupt teachers, such as Dumbledore during his welcoming speech, with her high-pitched girlish cough of "<i>Hem hem</i>" and speak to students in a condescending tone, as if they were simpletons or her inferiors; her personal speech during the Start-of-Term Feast already left a very negative first impression on the school in general, as most students could not be bothered to listen to the "load of waffle", while the teachers and Hermione Granger deduced the meaning that "the Ministry is interfering at Hogwarts", which displeased them. However, Dumbledore could not do anything about her due to her being appointed by the Ministry, and school life was made infinitely more difficult — for students and staff alike — by her presence.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3d/Umbridge_inspecting_Snape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150816123416" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Umbridge inspecting Snape.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge_inspecting_Snape.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3d/Umbridge_inspecting_Snape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150816123416" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3d/Umbridge_inspecting_Snape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150816123416" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3d/Umbridge_inspecting_Snape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150816123416" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Umbridge inspecting Snape.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge_inspecting_Snape.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3d/Umbridge_inspecting_Snape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150816123416" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Umbridge_inspecting_Snape.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Umbridge, as High Inquisitor, inspecting <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The students who despised her cruelty started a massive rebellion inspired by <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred</a> and <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George Weasley</a> after they set off a <a href="/wiki/Portable_Swamp" title="Portable Swamp">Portable Swamp</a> and fled the school. The teachers and staff, most of whom despised Umbridge's methods and interfering in their classes, did little to support her, and instead allowed the students to run rampant. Some of them were <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Filius Flitwick</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pomona_Sprout" title="Pomona Sprout">Pomona Sprout</a>, <a href="/wiki/Poppy_Pomfrey" title="Poppy Pomfrey">Poppy Pomfrey</a>, and even <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>. Madam Pomfrey however looked after her as she would any other following her rescue from the Centaurs.
</p><p>Umbridge was particularly offensive and prejudiced towards <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Hagrid</a>, due to his half-giant blood, and to <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Professor Trelawney</a>, who Umbridge believed was a fraud. Eventually, Umbridge sacked Trelawney and attempted to rudely evict her from the school, only to be foiled by Dumbledore. This also turned even more of the students and staff against her. In fact, the school itself appeared to deny her authority, sealing the Headmaster's office against her. In addition, Umbridge liked to intimidate <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Snape</a>, despite both of them sharing a dislike of Harry Potter. Unlike Trelawney, who took these horrible comments to heart and was deeply insulted, Snape rarely took any of her tauntings seriously. Besides, the staff, the students, and Peeves, the residents of the castle paintings also regarded her and her helpers with general distaste, swearing and making rude hand gestures at her and Cornelius Fudge when they left the Headmaster's office in pursuit of Dumbledore. Dobby was also terrified of her, warning of her approach to Harry in hysterics, and barely able to say her name.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Umbridge</b>: "<i>You're on Probation!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Severus Snape</b>: "<i>*looks back at her, his eyebrows slightly raised*</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Umbridge</b>: "<i>You are being deliberately unhelpful! I expected better, Lucius Malfoy always speaks most highly of you! Now get out of my office!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Umbridge's assessment of Snape after he tells her that he has no more <a href="/wiki/Veritaserum" title="Veritaserum">Veritaserum</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/B5C27M3_Dumbledore%27s_escape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180423215252" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B5C27M3 Dumbledore&#39;s escape.jpg" data-image-key="B5C27M3_Dumbledore&#39;s_escape.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/B5C27M3_Dumbledore%27s_escape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180423215252" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/B5C27M3_Dumbledore%27s_escape.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180423215252" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/B5C27M3_Dumbledore%27s_escape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180423215252" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B5C27M3 Dumbledore&#39;s escape.jpg" data-image-key="B5C27M3_Dumbledore&#39;s_escape.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/B5C27M3_Dumbledore%27s_escape.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180423215252" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B5C27M3_Dumbledore%27s_escape.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dumbledore after having incapacitated Umbridge and other Ministry officials</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Umbridge especially disliked <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, as he kept undermining her attempts to wrest control of <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. She, like <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a>, believed that Dumbledore was trying to overthrow the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> and hence usurp the position of <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Magic" title="Minister for Magic">Minister for Magic</a>. Of all, she was one of the only individuals who did the feat (and mistake) of angering Dumbledore when she attacked a student in front of him, a thing that even Voldemort himself was not able to do.
</p>
<h3><span id="Dumbledore's_Army"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Dumbledore.27s_Army">Dumbledore's Army</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=31" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Dumbledore&#039;s Army">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Dumbledore&#039;s Army"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>The purpose of Potter’s meeting with these students, was to persuade them to join an illegal society, whose aim was to learn <a href="/wiki/Spell" title="Spell">spells</a> and <a href="/wiki/Curse" title="Curse">curses</a> the Ministry has decided are inappropriate for school-age —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Umrbidge's condemnation of Dumbledore's Army<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161123060553" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="166" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore&#39;s Army.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore&#39;s_Army.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161123060553" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161123060553" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161123060553" decoding="async" width="250" height="166" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore&#39;s Army.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore&#39;s_Army.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161123060553" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>, Hogwarts students who rejected her authority and rebelled against her</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Dumbledore's Army was an organisation founded by <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> and led by Harry in order to teach the members <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a>, something that Umbridge didn't. Dumbledore's Army was also an organisation founded in order to directly oppose Umbridge and her supporters. When Umbridge found out about the organisation, she utilised the powers of <a href="/wiki/Educational_Decree_Number_Twenty-Four" title="Educational Decree Number Twenty-Four">Educational Decree Number Twenty-Four</a> to have them all expelled, but failed due to Dumbledore taking the blame.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>You <a href="/wiki/Hag" title="Hag">hag</a>, you evil hag! I know what you’re doing, you awful, twisted, vicious —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Hermione Granger's hatred of Umbridge<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Some of the members were: <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a>, <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>, <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred</a> and <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George Weasley</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ernest_Macmillan" title="Ernest Macmillan">Ernie Macmillan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Justin_Finch-Fletchley" title="Justin Finch-Fletchley">Justin Finch-Fletchley</a>, <a href="/wiki/Susan_Bones" title="Susan Bones">Susan Bones</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hannah_Abbott" title="Hannah Abbott">Hannah Abbott</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cho_Chang" title="Cho Chang">Cho Chang</a>, <a href="/wiki/Alicia_Spinnet" title="Alicia Spinnet">Alicia Spinnet</a>, <a href="/wiki/Katie_Bell" title="Katie Bell">Katie Bell</a>, <a href="/wiki/Angelina_Johnson" title="Angelina Johnson">Angelina Johnson</a>, <a href="/wiki/Colin_and_Dennis_Creevey" title="Colin and Dennis Creevey">Colin and Dennis Creevey</a>, <a href="/wiki/Michael_Corner" title="Michael Corner">Michael Corner</a>, <a href="/wiki/Terry_Boot" title="Terry Boot">Terry Boot</a>, <a href="/wiki/Anthony_Goldstein" title="Anthony Goldstein">Anthony Goldstein</a>, <a href="/wiki/Zacharias_Smith" title="Zacharias Smith">Zacharias Smith</a>, <a href="/wiki/Padma_and_Parvati_Patil" title="Padma and Parvati Patil">Padma and Parvati Patil</a> and <a href="/wiki/Marietta_Edgecombe" title="Marietta Edgecombe">Marietta Edgecombe</a>. All of them, aside from Marietta, disliked Umbridge. For instance, Hermione cited that she was an evil woman trying to dictate the affairs of the entire school, while Ron said she was "sick" in the head.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>However, Marietta betrayed the Army to Umbridge because of her parents' loyalty to the Ministry. Although Umbridge feigned kindness in encouraging Marietta to do "the right thing", when <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Shacklebolt" title="Kingsley Shacklebolt">Kingsley Shacklebolt</a> secretly modified Marietta's memory, Umbridge was furious with the young girl for being unable to answer her questions. This caused the High Inquisitor to violently shake Marietta until Dumbledore quickly stepped in.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Part-Humans_and_Muggle-Borns">Part-Humans and Muggle-Borns</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=32" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Part-Humans and Muggle-Borns">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Part-Humans and Muggle-Borns"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Filthy half-breeds! Beasts! Uncontrolled animals!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Umbridge insulting a herd of centaurs in fear<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Umbridge always had a prejudiced view on those who were part-humans. She used the derogatory term "<a href="/wiki/Half-breed" title="Half-breed">half-breed</a>" and treated them particularly horribly. This extended to creatures that looked like part-humans, but were in fact a separate breed, such as <a href="/wiki/Centaur" title="Centaur">centaurs</a>, <a href="/wiki/Merpeople" title="Merpeople">merpeople</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolves</a>, as she either mistook them to be human-animal hybrids or simply found their appearances of being partially human revolting. Regardless of her definition of "half-breeds", she was extremely cruel to them, writing an <a href="/wiki/Anti-werewolf_legislation" title="Anti-werewolf legislation">anti-werewolf legislation</a> so they could barely find employment, and campaigning for merpeople to be rounded up and tagged, the latter which was never followed through due to the sheer ridiculousness.
</p><p>In particular, Umbridge was horrible to <a href="/wiki/Half-giant" title="Half-giant">half-giant</a> <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a>, treating him like a dimwitted and violent <a href="/wiki/Troll" title="Troll">troll</a>, and ultimately tried to <a href="/wiki/Ousting_of_Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Ousting of Rubeus Hagrid">attack him under the cover of darkness</a>. Umbridge was also horrified at the appointment of the new <a href="/wiki/Divination" title="Divination">Divination</a> teacher, the centaur <a href="/wiki/Firenze" title="Firenze">Firenze</a>. Her prejudice eventually led her to foolishly insult and anger a herd of centaurs who dragged her away, which led her to develop a phobia towards centaurs.
</p><p>However, despite her hatred towards half-breeds, Umbridge did not seem to hate <a href="/wiki/Half-goblin" title="Half-goblin">part-goblin</a> <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Filius Flitwick</a>, judging by <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred Weasley</a>'s statement that she passed him on his inspection. Although this is most likely a result of Umbridge's lack of knowledge on Flitwick's ancestry. Alternatively, it is possible that Flitwick's all-around competence led to her being unable to find a pretext to mark him down.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b1/Trial1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150816122531" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Trial1.jpg" data-image-key="Trial1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b1/Trial1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150816122531" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b1/Trial1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150816122531" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b1/Trial1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150816122531" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Trial1.jpg" data-image-key="Trial1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b1/Trial1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150816122531" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Trial1.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Umbridge's hatred extending to Muggle-borns</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>One year before she was incarcerated in <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a>, Umbridge's cruel prejudice extended to <a href="/wiki/Muggle-borns" class="mw-redirect" title="Muggle-borns">Muggle-borns</a>, due to her hypocritical-conformity of the ideology of <a href="/wiki/Blood_status" title="Blood status">blood purity</a>.
</p><p>She sadistically interrogated them alongside <a href="/wiki/Corban_Yaxley" title="Corban Yaxley">Yaxley</a>, two prime victims being <a href="/wiki/Alderton" title="Alderton">Alderton</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mary_Cattermole" title="Mary Cattermole">Mary Cattermole</a>. She also published a pamphlet stating the dangers of Muggles and referred to them as "<a href="/wiki/Mudblood" title="Mudblood">Mudbloods</a>". Her crimes against Muggle-borns led to her imprisonment in Azkaban following the defeat of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>, especially since some of the Muggle-borns she convicted did not survive Azkaban.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermoreprofile_1-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermoreprofile-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Death_Eaters">Death Eaters</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=33" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Death Eaters">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Death Eaters"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/Unidentified_Death_Eater_%28II%29.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20091129164509" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="247" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Unidentified Death Eater (II).jpg" data-image-key="Unidentified_Death_Eater_(II).jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/Unidentified_Death_Eater_%28II%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20091129164509" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/Unidentified_Death_Eater_%28II%29.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20091129164509" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/Unidentified_Death_Eater_%28II%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20091129164509" decoding="async" width="180" height="247" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Unidentified Death Eater (II).jpg" data-image-key="Unidentified_Death_Eater_(II).jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6c/Unidentified_Death_Eater_%28II%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20091129164509" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Unidentified_Death_Eater_(II).jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A masked Death Eater</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Although Umbridge was not a Death Eater, and had no direct contact with <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>, she showed that she was fairly in line with their goals. This was due to Umbridge's callous nature, prejudiced beliefs (both of which were similar to Death Eater behaviour) and her antagonism and disrespect to <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, whom she tried to hinder or thwart on several occasions. Umbridge seemed to be on friendly terms with <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a>, a known Death Eater who had close connections with the Ministry.
</p><p>In addition, Umbridge was seen working alongside <a href="/wiki/Corban_Yaxley" title="Corban Yaxley">Yaxley</a>, another Death Eater, who was part of the <a href="/wiki/Muggle-Born_Registration_Commission" title="Muggle-Born Registration Commission">Muggle-Born Registration Commission</a> which Umbridge was in charge of. Umbridge's duties as the head of this commission involved sadistically prosecuting innocent Muggle-borns who were the enemies of the Death Eaters. However, Umbridge was never actually part of Lord Voldemort's ring of Death Eaters, although it appears that with her <a href="/wiki/Mudbloods_and_the_Dangers_They_Pose_to_a_Peaceful_Pure-Blood_Society" title="Mudbloods and the Dangers They Pose to a Peaceful Pure-Blood Society">Mudblood prejudice leaflet</a>, she supported Muggle-born segregation. While Umbridge was never known to have joined Voldemort, or been aware of his infiltration of the Ministry in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, her displayed behaviour suggests that she had no problems with the changes that he introduced.
</p><p>In an alternative reality where Voldemort succeeded in conquering Britain and killing Harry, Dolores was full-heartedly celebrating "Voldemort Day", showing she was aware of the Death Eaters taking over, and her full and open support for Lord Voldemort.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Media">Media</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=34" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Media">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Media"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=35" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Etymology"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Dolores<i> is a common Spanish name, although it also occurs as an English name. In Spanish and Latin, "dolores" is also the plural form of "dolor", which means pain. In English, the similar sounding word "Dolorous" means causing or expressing grief and suffering. Dolor is the Danish name of the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a>.</i>
</p>
<ul><li>Jane is a sweet name for a girl, adding a cruel irony to her nomenclature. Because her middle name is "Jane," J.K. Rowling changed <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>'s middle name (which was also Jane) to "Jean" in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows</a></i>.</li>
<li>"Umbridge" is a pun on the English "umbrage" meaning "offence" or "insult", indicates that Dolores Umbridge is destined to do only harm and cause only unhappiness. It also symbolises how she is offended by any challenge to her limited world-view and her secretive nature. "Umbrage", which came from the Middle French "ombrage" and ultimately from the Latin "umbra" is a word whose meaning has evolved over time. Originally, "Umbrage" meant "shadow" or "shade", then it evolved to refer to "that which provides shadow or shade", then took on the meaning "semblance" or "suspicion", and eventually to "the suspicion that one has been slighted" and its present meaning.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Behind_the_scenes">Behind the scenes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=36" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Behind the scenes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Behind the scenes"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
