<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Dolores_Umbridge_game.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130415154002" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="202" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dolores Umbridge game.jpg" data-image-key="Dolores_Umbridge_game.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Dolores_Umbridge_game.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130415154002" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Dolores_Umbridge_game.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130415154002" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Dolores_Umbridge_game.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130415154002" decoding="async" width="180" height="202" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dolores Umbridge game.jpg" data-image-key="Dolores_Umbridge_game.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Dolores_Umbridge_game.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130415154002" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dolores_Umbridge_game.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dolores Umbridge in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(video_game)" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (video game)">Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (video game)</a></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/Umbridge_LEGO.png/revision/latest?cb=20190510125841" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="254" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Umbridge LEGO.png" data-image-key="Umbridge_LEGO.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/Umbridge_LEGO.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190510125841" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/Umbridge_LEGO.png/revision/latest?cb=20190510125841" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/Umbridge_LEGO.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190510125841" decoding="async" width="180" height="254" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Umbridge LEGO.png" data-image-key="Umbridge_LEGO.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/Umbridge_LEGO.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190510125841" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Umbridge_LEGO.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dolores Umbridge in <i><a href="/wiki/LEGO_Harry_Potter:_Years_5-7" title="LEGO Harry Potter: Years 5-7">LEGO Harry Potter: Years 5-7</a></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Umbridge_Pop.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190510125744" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="127" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Umbridge Pop.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge_Pop.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Umbridge_Pop.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190510125744" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Umbridge_Pop.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190510125744" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Umbridge_Pop.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190510125744" decoding="async" width="180" height="127" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Umbridge Pop.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge_Pop.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Umbridge_Pop.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190510125744" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Umbridge_Pop.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dolores Umbridge as a <a href="/wiki/POP!_Vinyl" title="POP! Vinyl">POP! Vinyl</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/14/Lola.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100620105950" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Lola.jpg" data-image-key="Lola.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/14/Lola.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100620105950" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/14/Lola.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100620105950" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/14/Lola.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100620105950" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Lola.jpg" data-image-key="Lola.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/14/Lola.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100620105950" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Lola.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dolores as a LEGO minifugre (2007 edition)</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 172px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2a/LLEGOUmbridge.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190904200135" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="170" height="253" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="LLEGOUmbridge.jpg" data-image-key="LLEGOUmbridge.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2a/LLEGOUmbridge.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/170?cb=20190904200135" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2a/LLEGOUmbridge.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190904200135" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2a/LLEGOUmbridge.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/170?cb=20190904200135" decoding="async" width="170" height="253" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="LLEGOUmbridge.jpg" data-image-key="LLEGOUmbridge.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2a/LLEGOUmbridge.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/170?cb=20190904200135" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:LLEGOUmbridge.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dolores as a LEGO minifigure (2018 edition)</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>Umbridge is portrayed by <a href="/wiki/Great_Britain" title="Great Britain">British</a> actress <a href="/wiki/Imelda_Staunton" title="Imelda Staunton">Imelda Staunton</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix</a></i> and the first part of the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_1" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 1">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Of the seven Defence Against the Dark Arts teachers over the time when the series is set, Umbridge is the only woman to hold the post.</li>
<li>It has been noted by many fans, Imelda Staunton and even <a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> herself that Dolores bears many similarities to the late Prime Minister Margaret Thatcher. Who, similar to Umbridge, was minister for education, and made many changes that the public disagreed with (though ironically she was the one to ban the cane in British schools), and was also known for her soft approach when addressing the public, but was also known for being radical, harsh and in some cases extreme with her polices and methods in running the country during her tenure.</li>
<li>The power granted to Umbridge by Fudge to consolidate his political strength and squash his perceived enemies is not unlike the abuse members of the Nixon administration committed during the Watergate Era. In addition, Umbridge's final crimes are the "ethnic cleansing" of Muggle-born wizards, analogous to the Nazi persecutions leading to the Holocaust.</li>
<li>Actress Staunton said that she nearly vomited when she had filmed the scene where Umbridge makes Harry write in his own blood during his fifth year. She also said that it was amongst the most "<i>sickening parts she ever filmed</i>".</li>
<li>Professor Umbridge is one of the least popular <i>Harry Potter</i> characters in the opinions of the main characters. However, Neville Longbottom has stated that she was significantly less harsh than the Carrows, as she did not directly use dark magic. J. K. Rowling herself has noted that Umbridge is "<i>a nasty piece of work</i>". David Yates also described her as a splice between Doris Day and Freddy Krueger.
<ul><li>Likewise, in the real world, Umbridge is arguably the most hated character in the entire franchise, well ahead of <a href="/wiki/Alecto_and_Amycus_Carrow" title="Alecto and Amycus Carrow">the Carrows</a>, <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rita_Skeeter" title="Rita Skeeter">Rita Skeeter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Argus_Filch" title="Argus Filch">Argus Filch</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>, <a href="/wiki/Zacharias_Smith" title="Zacharias Smith">Zacharias Smith</a>, <a href="/wiki/Romilda_Vane" title="Romilda Vane">Romilda Vane</a>,Marietta Edgecombe, <a href="/wiki/Marjorie_Dursley" title="Marjorie Dursley">Marjorie Dursley</a>,<a href="/wiki/Vinda_Rosier" title="Vinda Rosier">Vinda Rosier</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mary_Lou_Barebone" title="Mary Lou Barebone">Mary Lou Barebone</a> and even Voldemort himself. Ironically, <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a> claimed that the Carrows <i>"make her look tame"</i>.</li></ul></li>
<li>Despite Professor McGonagall's hatred for Umbridge, they share the same patronus form: a cat. Both of their Patronuses are shown in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows</a></i>.</li>
<li>Horror novelist <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stephen_King" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Stephen King">Stephen King</a> (a great fan of <a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a>), writing as a book reviewer for the <a href="/wiki/11_July" title="11 July">11 July</a>, <a href="/wiki/2003" title="2003">2003</a> <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Entertainment_Weekly" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Entertainment Weekly">Entertainment Weekly</a>, noted that "the success of any fantasy novel depends on a great villain", and called Umbridge the "<i>greatest make-believe villain to come along since Hannibal Lecter</i>".<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>The <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener" class="external text" href="https://harrypotter.fandom.com/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(film)">film adaptation</a> of <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener" class="external text" href="https://harrypotter.fandom.com/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix">Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix​</a> omits the detail that Umbridge was the person who sent the <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a> to attack Harry, nor does it identify the one who was responsible. It is implied however, that she was the one who sent them to attack Harry when she attempts to use the Cruciatus Curse on Harry later on in the film.</li>
<li>In the fifth film adaptation, Umbridge does not say Harry Potter's first name at all. She does use the name "Potter" when saying his surname or calling him "Mr Potter" when addressing Harry and she only 'says' it when her actor Imelda Staunton is in an interview of Disc 2 Special Features.</li>
<li>Umbridge may be related to Death Eater <a href="/wiki/Selwyn" title="Selwyn">Selwyn</a>, as she claimed in <i>Deathly Hallows</i> that she was related to the <a href="/wiki/Selwyn_family" title="Selwyn family">Selwyn family</a>, though this is a lie to "bolster her own <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood" title="Pure-blood">pure-blood</a> credentials", because she has a <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">muggle</a> mother and so is definitely a <a href="/wiki/Half-blood" title="Half-blood">half-blood</a>.</li>
<li>Interestingly enough, when she finds Hermione (disguised as Mafalda Hopkirk), she says "<i><a href="/wiki/Travers" title="Travers">Travers</a> sent you, did he?</i>" Travers is also a Death Eater. Perhaps by coincidence, Travers and Selwyn are the two Death Eaters that attack Harry, Ron, and Hermione when they go to see <a href="/wiki/Xenophilius_Lovegood" title="Xenophilius Lovegood">Xenophilius Lovegood</a>.</li>
<li>The only staff member to ever like Umbridge was <a href="/wiki/Argus_Filch" title="Argus Filch">Argus Filch</a>, who thought she was the best thing to happen to Hogwarts. This was mostly since she gave him powers over students to whip them or hang them by their ankles in exchange for him spying for her.</li>
<li>In the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince</a></i>, there is a <a href="/wiki/Umbridge_on_Unicycle" title="Umbridge on Unicycle">figure</a> of Umbridge balancing on a rope shouting "<i>I really hate children</i>." and "<i>I will have order!</i>" repeatedly in the <a href="/wiki/Weasleys%27_Wizard_Wheezes" title="Weasleys&#39; Wizard Wheezes">Weasleys' Wizard Wheezes</a> Joke Shop. This is weird as <a href="/wiki/Fred_and_George_Weasley" title="Fred and George Weasley">Fred and George Weasley</a> weren't in the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a> to hear these lines. However, a possible explanation is that Umbridge actually says these two lines frequently.</li>
<li>According to <a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a>, in early drafts of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix</a></i>, Umbridge's first name was Elvira.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Despite her hatred towards <a href="/wiki/Half-breed" title="Half-breed">half-breeds</a>, Umbridge did not seem to hate part-goblin <a href="/wiki/Filius_Flitwick" title="Filius Flitwick">Filius Flitwick</a>, as <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred Weasley</a> stated that she marked him well on his inspection (this may be due to the fact that the goblin blood comes from a distant ancestor). In the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix</a></i> however, she does harass Flitwick by measuring him, as if there is a height requirement. Most likely this was an exercise in making herself feel better about her own short stature.</li>
<li>In the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix</a></i>, Umbridge is shown with blue eyes, but in the book she is described to have "slitted brown" eyes.</li>
<li>In the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_1" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 1">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 1</a></i>, Umbridge's Kitten Brooch and Ring were custom-made by Israeli jewellery designer <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener" class="external text" href="http://www.michalnegrin.com/">Michal Negrin,</a> who then subsequently made a small collection of pieces with a similar pattern.</li>
<li>In the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_1_(video_game)" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 1 (video game)"><i>Deathly Hallows Part 1</i> video game</a>, the <i><a href="/wiki/Expulso_Curse" title="Expulso Curse">Expulso</a></i> <a href="/wiki/Expulso_spellbook" title="Expulso spellbook">spellbook</a> is in her office, squarely in the centre of her desktop. It is not elaborated on why she possessed this item, though it is quite possible that she'd confiscated it. It is also possible that it was actually hers, since her magical power was concentrated in offensive and defensive magic.</li>
<li>The influence of the Locket on Umbridge is notably similar to the influence of the <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Three_Rings#Nenya" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Three Rings">Ring of Power</a> on Galadriel, in that both experienced amplified magical power and malice. Both were also being influenced by the rehoused soul of a Dark wizard, more or less (although, unlike Galadriel, Umbridge was already evil).</li>
<li>In <i><a href="/wiki/LEGO_Harry_Potter:_Years_5-7" title="LEGO Harry Potter: Years 5-7">LEGO Harry Potter: Years 5-7</a></i>, Umbridge is seen to have great evasion, as she is capable of performing flips while fighting against centaurs in the episode "A Giant Virtuoso". She also has the habit to <a href="/wiki/Book_transfiguring_spell" title="Book transfiguring spell">change books</a> about offensive use of spells into pink books about cats, much to students' irritation. Also, during <a href="/wiki/Mary_Cattermole" title="Mary Cattermole">Mary Cattermole</a>'s judgement in the <a href="/wiki/Wizengamot" title="Wizengamot">Wizengamot</a> room, instead of being knocked by Harry Potter at the first time, she and <a href="/wiki/Corban_Yaxley" title="Corban Yaxley">Corban Yaxley</a> fought Potter, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ronald Weasley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> in the room with a parody of the <a href="/wiki/Reverse_Spell" title="Reverse Spell">Reverse Spell</a>. The fight ended after Umbridge was knocked and fell into her judge seat.</li>
<li>In the film adaptations, her hairstyle bears a resemblance to that of Margaret Thatcher, a controversial former British Prime Minister.</li>
<li>In the "The Lizzie Bennet Diaries", an Emmy-winning YouTube vlog that is a modern version of <i>Pride and Prejudice</i>, Ashley Clemmets (Lizzie Bennet) used Umbridge as an inspiration to perform Lady Catherine De Bough in several of the episodes throughout the series.</li>
<li>Much of her tyrannical rise to power was shown, as she wanted to cast a Cruciatus Curse on Harry, an Unforgivable Curse. It is unknown how much the spell would be painful to Harry, but, when taking into consideration her nature, the spell would be almost as powerful as Bellatrix Lestrange's Cruciatus Curse.</li>
<li>Gillian Berrow, a story writer for the television series My Little Pony Friendship is Magic, has stated that Umbridge was a model for the villainous MLP character Starlight Glimmer.</li>
<li>In the German audio books, Dolores Umbridge has an Austrian accent.</li>
<li>Umbridge's wand being of Birch wood is a reference to the practice of birching, a corporal punishment where a victim is beaten with a birch rod.</li>
<li>Dolores Umbridge is essentially a dark reflection of <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ronald Weasley</a>. Both of them were implied to have lonely pre-Hogwarts lives and they felt overshadowed by their family and resented that the school did not grant them any position of power and responsibility. Both of them were loyal to the <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Magic" title="Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> and had a father that worked there; both of their fathers were of low rank (janitor and <a href="/wiki/Misuse_of_Muggle_Artefacts_Office" title="Misuse of Muggle Artefacts Office">Misuse of Muggle Artefacts Office</a>, respectively), which they were both implied (in both cases without any cemented evidence) to be insecure about. They were both forced to wear <a href="/wiki/Slytherin%27s_Locket" title="Slytherin&#39;s Locket">Slytherin's Locket</a>, which exacerbated their worst traits such as selfishness and selective loyalty. But the difference is that, as <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> once cited, Umbridge's darker traits took over her mind, while Ron chose to turn over a fresh leaf and eventually got the position of power he wanted, choosing to act on the light in him.</li>
<li>It sounds inconsistent Harry to notice in <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">The Order of the Phoenix novel</a>, that Dolores "<i>obviously did not know how things were done at Hogwarts</i>" as no new teacher had ever interrupted Dumbledore before, implying that Dolores had never been at Hogwarts.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP11_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP11-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> Despite that, later is revealed in  <i><a href="/wiki/Pottermore" title="Pottermore">Pottermore</a></i> that she is graduated there.<sup id="cite_ref-birth_2-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-birth-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Long-time personal correspondant of J. K. Rowling and Master of Horror Stephen King, who created terrifying creatures like Pennywise, Cujo, Christine, and the Tommyknockers, said in his review of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix</a></i> that Umbridge was the scariest villain since <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hannibal_Lecter" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Hannibal Lecter">Hannibal Lecter</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span id="Author's_comments"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Author.27s_comments">Author's comments</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?veaction=edit&amp;section=37" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Author&#039;s comments">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge?action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Author&#039;s comments"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b1/PinkUmbridge.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170115110933" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="PinkUmbridge.jpg" data-image-key="PinkUmbridge.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b1/PinkUmbridge.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170115110933" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b1/PinkUmbridge.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170115110933" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b1/PinkUmbridge.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170115110933" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="PinkUmbridge.jpg" data-image-key="PinkUmbridge.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b1/PinkUmbridge.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170115110933" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:PinkUmbridge.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Devil wears pink</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>"<i>Once, long ago, I took instruction in a certain skill or subject (I am being vague as vague can be, for reasons that are about to become obvious), and in doing so, came into contact with a teacher or instructor whom I disliked intensely on sight.</i>
</p><p><i>The woman in question returned my antipathy with interest. Why we took against each other so instantly, heartily and (on my side, at least) irrationally, I honestly cannot say. What sticks in my mind is her pronounced taste for twee accessories. I particularly recall a tiny little plastic bow slide, pale lemon in colour that she wore in her short curly hair. I used to stare at that little slide, which would have been appropriate to a girl of three, as though it was some kind of repellant physical growth. She was quite a stocky woman, and not in the first flush of youth, and her tendency to wear frills where (I felt) frills had no business to be, and to carry undersized handbags, again as though they had been borrowed from a child's dressing-up box, jarred, I felt, with a personality that I found the reverse of sweet, innocent, and ingenuous.</i>
</p><p><i>I am always a little wary when talking about these kinds of sources of inspiration, because it is infuriating to hear yourself misinterpreted in ways that can cause other people a great deal of hurt. This woman was NOT 'the real Dolores Umbridge'. She did not look like a toad, she was never sadistic or vicious to me or anyone else, and I never heard her express a single view in common with Umbridge (indeed, I never knew her well enough to know much about her views or preferences, which makes my dislike of her even less justifiable). However, it is true to say that I borrowed from her, then grossly exaggerated, a taste for the sickly sweet and girlish in dress, and it was that tiny little pale lemon plastic bow that I was remembering when I perched the fly-like ornament on Dolores Umbridge's head.</i>
</p><p><i>I have noticed more than once in life that a taste for the ineffably twee can go hand-in-hand with a distinctly uncharitable outlook on the world. I once shared an office with a woman who had covered the wall space behind her desk with pictures of fluffy kitties; she was the most bigoted, spiteful champion of the death penalty with whom it has ever been my misfortune to share a kettle. A love of all things saccharine often seems present where there is a lack of real warmth or charity.</i>
</p><p><i>So Dolores, who is one of the characters for whom I feel purest dislike, became an amalgam of traits taken from these, and a variety of sources. Her desire to control, to punish and to inflict pain, all in the name of law and order, are, I think, every bit as reprehensible as Lord Voldemort's unvarnished espousal of evil.</i>
</p><p><i>Umbridge's names were carefully chosen. 'Dolores' means sorrow, something she undoubtedly inflicts on all around her. 'Umbridge' is a play on 'umbrage' from the British expression 'to take umbrage', meaning offence. Dolores is offended by any challenge to her limited world-view; I felt her surname conveyed the pettiness and rigidity of her character. It is harder to explain 'Jane'; it simply felt rather smug and neat between her other two names.</i>"
</p>
